===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/agents/orchestrator.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/agents/orchestrator.py
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from typing import Any, Dict

from langgraph.graph import StateGraph, END
from langgraph.checkpoint.memory import MemorySaver

from ..state import ConsultState
from ..nodes.lite_router import lite_router_node
from ..nodes.intent_llm import intent_router_node
from ..nodes.smalltalk import smalltalk_node
from ...logging_utils import wrap_node_with_logging

from .material_agent import build_material_agent_subgraph
from .application_agent import build_application_agent_subgraph
from .norms_agent import build_norms_agent_subgraph
from .product_market_agent import build_product_market_agent_subgraph
from .safety_agent import safety_agent_node
from .value_chain_agent import build_value_chain_agent_subgraph

log = logging.getLogger("uvicorn.error")
_ORCHESTRATOR_NAME = "Orchestrator"

def _route_to_agent(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    """
    Route to appropriate agent based on domain/intent.
    """
    domain = (state.get("domain") or "").strip().lower()
    intent = (state.get("route") or "").strip().lower()

    if intent in {"chitchat", "smalltalk"}:
        return "smalltalk"
    elif domain == "rwdr" or "material" in intent:
        return "material_agent"
    elif "application" in intent or "mechanical" in intent:
        return "application_agent"
    elif "norm" in intent or "compliance" in intent:
        return "norms_agent"
    elif "product" in intent or "market" in intent:
        return "product_market_agent"
    elif "value" in intent or "chain" in intent or "stakeholder" in intent:
        return "value_chain_agent"
    else:
        return "material_agent"  # Default

def build_orchestrator_graph(checkpointer=None) -> StateGraph:
    """
    Main orchestrator graph that routes to agent subgraphs.
    """
    g = StateGraph(ConsultState)

    # Subgraphs
    material_sg = build_material_agent_subgraph(checkpointer)
    application_sg = build_application_agent_subgraph(checkpointer)
    norms_sg = build_norms_agent_subgraph(checkpointer)
    product_market_sg = build_product_market_agent_subgraph(checkpointer)
    value_chain_sg = build_value_chain_agent_subgraph(checkpointer)

    # Nodes
    g.add_node("lite_router", wrap_node_with_logging(_ORCHESTRATOR_NAME, "lite_router", lite_router_node))
    g.add_node("intent_router", intent_router_node)
    g.add_node("smalltalk", wrap_node_with_logging(_ORCHESTRATOR_NAME, "smalltalk", smalltalk_node))
    g.add_node("material_agent", material_sg)
    g.add_node("application_agent", application_sg)
    g.add_node("norms_agent", norms_sg)
    g.add_node("product_market_agent", product_market_sg)
    g.add_node("value_chain_agent", value_chain_sg)
    g.add_node("safety_check", wrap_node_with_logging(_ORCHESTRATOR_NAME, "safety_check", safety_agent_node))

    # Edges
    g.set_entry_point("lite_router")
    g.add_conditional_edges("lite_router", lambda s: (s.get("route") or "default").strip().lower(), {
        "smalltalk": "smalltalk",
        "default": "intent_router",
    })
    g.add_conditional_edges("intent_router", _route_to_agent, {
        "smalltalk": "smalltalk",
        "material_agent": "material_agent",
        "application_agent": "application_agent",
        "norms_agent": "norms_agent",
        "product_market_agent": "product_market_agent",
        "value_chain_agent": "value_chain_agent",
    })
    g.add_edge("smalltalk", END)

    # After each agent, safety check
    for agent in ["material_agent", "application_agent", "norms_agent", "product_market_agent", "value_chain_agent"]:
        g.add_edge(agent, "safety_check")
    g.add_edge("safety_check", END)

    if checkpointer is None:
        checkpointer = MemorySaver()
    compiled = g.compile(checkpointer=checkpointer)
    log.info("[Orchestrator] Graph compiled")
    return compiled
===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/agents/orchestrator.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/agents/orchestrator.py =====

def _after_validate_answer(state: Dict[str, Any], agent: str) -> str:
    """
    Agent-specific routing after validate_answer.
    For product/market agent, focus on market trends and search accuracy.
    """

        return "ask_missing"

    revise_count = int((state.get("metrics") or {}).get("revise_count", 0))
    if conf < 0.65 and revise_count < 2:  # Lower threshold for broad market data
        return "critique"
    return "respond"

# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/agents/product_market_agent.py

from langgraph.checkpoint.memory import MemorySaver

    _ask_or_ok, _after_rag, _critique_key, _bump_revise_count_node

    # Nodes
    g.add_node("intake", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "intake", intake_node))
    g.add_node("extract", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "extract", _extract_node))
    g.add_node("compute", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "compute", _compute_node))
    g.add_node("validate", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "validate", validate_node))
    g.add_node("prepare_query", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "prepare_query", _prepare_query_node))
    g.add_node("ltm", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "ltm", ltm_node))
    g.add_node("rag", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "rag", run_rag_node))  # Will integrate GraphRAG later
    g.add_node("recommend", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "recommend", recommend_node))
    g.add_node("validate_answer", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "validate_answer", validate_answer))
    g.add_node("explain", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "explain", explain_node))
    g.add_node("critique", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "critique", critique_node))
    g.add_node("respond", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "respond", _respond_node))
    g.add_node("summarize", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "summarize", summarize_node))
    g.add_node("bump_revise_count", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "bump_revise_count", _bump_revise_count_node))

    # Edges
    g.set_entry_point("intake")
    g.add_edge("intake", "extract")
    g.add_edge("extract", "compute")
    g.add_edge("compute", "validate")
    g.add_edge("validate", "prepare_query")
    g.add_edge("prepare_query", "ltm")
    g.add_edge("ltm", "rag")
    g.add_conditional_edges("rag", _after_rag, {"recommend": "recommend", "explain": "explain"})
    g.add_edge("recommend", "validate_answer")
    g.add_conditional_edges("validate_answer", lambda s: _after_validate_answer(s, agent="product_market"), {
        "ask_missing": "respond",
        "critique": "critique",
        "respond": "respond",
    })
    g.add_conditional_edges("critique", _critique_key, {
        "ask_missing": "respond",
        "revise": "bump_revise_count",
        "ok": "respond",
    })
    g.add_edge("bump_revise_count", "recommend")
    g.add_edge("explain", "critique")
    g.add_edge("respond", "summarize")
    g.add_edge("summarize", END)

    if checkpointer is None:
        checkpointer = MemorySaver()
    compiled = g.compile(checkpointer=checkpointer)
    log.info("[ProductMarketAgent] Subgraph compiled")
    return compiled

def _after_validate_answer(state: Dict[str, Any], agent: str) -> str:
    """
    Agent-specific routing after validate_answer.
    For product/market agent, focus on market trends and search accuracy.
    """
    if state.get("needs_more_params"):
        return "ask_missing"
    conf = float(state.get("confidence") or 0.0)
    revise_count = int((state.get("metrics") or {}).get("revise_count", 0))
    if conf < 0.65 and revise_count < 2:  # Lower threshold for broad market data
        return "critique"
    return "respond"
===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/agents/product_market_agent.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/agents/safety_agent.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/agents/safety_agent.py
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from typing import Any, Dict

from langchain_core.messages import AIMessage

from ..state import ConsultState
from ..config import create_llm

log = logging.getLogger("uvicorn.error")

def safety_agent_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Safety-Agent: Checks for bias in recommendations and performs adaptive learning.
    """
    try:
        recommendation = state.get("answer", "")
        params = state.get("params", {})
        domain = state.get("domain", "general")

        # Simple bias check prompt
        prompt = f"""
        Analyze the following recommendation for potential biases, inaccuracies, or safety concerns:
        Recommendation: {recommendation}
        Parameters: {params}
        Domain: {domain}

        Provide a bias score (0-1, where 0 is unbiased) and suggest improvements if biased.
        """

        llm = create_llm(streaming=False)
        resp = llm.invoke([{"role": "user", "content": prompt}])
        content = getattr(resp, "content", "").strip()

        # Parse score (simple)
        bias_score = 0.1  # Default low
        if "score" in content.lower():
            import re
            match = re.search(r'score[:\s]*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', content, re.IGNORECASE)
            if match:
                bias_score = float(match.group(1))

        # If biased, flag
        if bias_score > 0.3:
            log.warning("[SafetyAgent] High bias detected: %.2f", bias_score)
            # Could trigger revision, but for now just log

        return {
            **state,
            "bias_score": bias_score,
            "safety_check": content,
            "messages": state.get("messages", []) + [AIMessage(content=f"Safety Check: {content[:200]}...")],
        }
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[SafetyAgent] Error: %s", e)
        return {**state, "bias_score": 0.0, "safety_check": "Error in safety check."}
===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/agents/safety_agent.py =====

from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from typing import Any, Dict

from langgraph.graph import StateGraph, END
from langgraph.checkpoint.memory import MemorySaver

from ..state import ConsultState
from ..utils.graph_helpers import (
    _extract_node, _compute_node, _prepare_query_node, _respond_node,
    _ask_or_ok, _after_rag, _critique_key, _bump_revise_count_node
)
from ..nodes.intake import intake_node
from ..nodes.validate import validate_node
from ..nodes.recommend import recommend_node
from ..nodes.explain import explain_node
from ..nodes.critique import critique_node
from ..nodes.rag import run_rag_node
from ..nodes.ltm import ltm_node
from ..nodes.validate_answer import validate_answer
from ..nodes.summarize import summarize_node
from ...logging_utils import wrap_node_with_logging

log = logging.getLogger("uvicorn.error")
_AGENT_NAME = "ValueChainAgent"

def build_value_chain_agent_subgraph(checkpointer=None) -> StateGraph:
    """
    Subgraph for Value Chain/Stakeholder-Agent: Focuses on end-to-end processes, with self-critique.
    """
    g = StateGraph(ConsultState)

    # Nodes
    g.add_node("intake", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "intake", intake_node))
    g.add_node("extract", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "extract", _extract_node))
    g.add_node("compute", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "compute", _compute_node))
    g.add_node("validate", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "validate", validate_node))
    g.add_node("prepare_query", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "prepare_query", _prepare_query_node))
    g.add_node("ltm", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "ltm", ltm_node))
    g.add_node("rag", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "rag", run_rag_node))
    g.add_node("recommend", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "recommend", recommend_node))
    g.add_node("validate_answer", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "validate_answer", validate_answer))
    g.add_node("explain", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "explain", explain_node))
    g.add_node("critique", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "critique", critique_node))
    g.add_node("respond", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "respond", _respond_node))
    g.add_node("summarize", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "summarize", summarize_node))
    g.add_node("bump_revise_count", wrap_node_with_logging(_AGENT_NAME, "bump_revise_count", _bump_revise_count_node))

    # Edges
    g.set_entry_point("intake")
    g.add_edge("intake", "extract")
    g.add_edge("extract", "compute")
    g.add_edge("compute", "validate")
    g.add_edge("validate", "prepare_query")
    g.add_edge("prepare_query", "ltm")
    g.add_edge("ltm", "rag")
    g.add_conditional_edges("rag", _after_rag, {"recommend": "recommend", "explain": "explain"})
    g.add_edge("recommend", "validate_answer")
    g.add_conditional_edges("validate_answer", lambda s: _after_validate_answer(s, agent="value_chain"), {
        "ask_missing": "respond",
        "critique": "critique",
        "respond": "respond",
    })
    g.add_conditional_edges("critique", _critique_key, {
        "ask_missing": "respond",
        "revise": "bump_revise_count",
        "ok": "respond",
    })
    g.add_edge("bump_revise_count", "recommend")
    g.add_edge("explain", "critique")
    g.add_edge("respond", "summarize")
    g.add_edge("summarize", END)

    if checkpointer is None:
        checkpointer = MemorySaver()
    compiled = g.compile(checkpointer=checkpointer)
    log.info("[ValueChainAgent] Subgraph compiled")
    return compiled

def _after_validate_answer(state: Dict[str, Any], agent: str) -> str:
    """
    Agent-specific routing after validate_answer.
    For value chain agent, focus on holistic process validation.
    """
    if state.get("needs_more_params"):
        return "ask_missing"
    conf = float(state.get("confidence") or 0.0)
    revise_count = int((state.get("metrics") or {}).get("revise_count", 0))
    if conf < 0.7 and revise_count < 2:
        return "critique"
    return "respond"

# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/config.py
from __future__ import annotations

import os
from typing import Optional
from langchain_openai import ChatOpenAI  # FIX: Import für echtes Runnable

def create_llm(streaming: bool = False, model: str = "gpt-4o-mini") -> ChatOpenAI:
    """
    Erstellt ein LangChain LLM-Objekt (ChatOpenAI).
    FIX: Returned ein echtes Runnable statt Dict (z.B. Config).
    """
    api_key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY")
    if not api_key:
        raise ValueError("OPENAI_API_KEY not set")
    
    llm = ChatOpenAI(
        model=model,
        api_key=api_key,
        temperature=0.1,  # Deterministisch für Consult
        streaming=streaming,
    )
    return llm

# Alternative für get_default_llm (falls in ask_missing.py verwendet)
def get_default_llm(stream: Optional[bool] = False) -> ChatOpenAI:
    """
    FIX: Unterstützt 'stream' Arg und returned Runnable.
    """
    return create_llm(streaming=stream)

# Configurable constants
MAX_REVISE_COUNT = int(os.getenv('CONSULT_MAX_REVISE_COUNT', '2'))
RECURSION_LIMIT = int(os.getenv('CONSULT_RECURSION_LIMIT', '12'))
CRITIQUE_THRESHOLD = float(os.getenv('CONSULT_CRITIQUE_THRESHOLD', '0.8'))

# Domains config
DOMAINS = {
    'rwdr': {
        'name': 'RWDR',
        'description': 'RWDR Dichtungen'
    },
    'hydraulics_rod': {
        'name': 'Hydraulik Stangendichtung',
        'description': 'Hydraulik Stangendichtungen'
    }
}

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/config.py =====

===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/domain_router.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/domain_router.py
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional

from app.services.langgraph.graph.consult import utils as utils_mod

log = logging.getLogger("uvicorn.error")

def detect_domain(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[str]:
    """
    Heuristische Domain-Erkennung basierend auf params/messages im state.
    """
    params = state.get("params", {}) if state else {}
    msgs = utils_mod.normalize_messages(state.get("messages", [])) if state else []

    text_parts = []
    for v in params.values():
        if isinstance(v, str):
            text_parts.append(v)
    for m in msgs:
        try:
            c = getattr(m, "content", "") or ""
            if isinstance(c, str):
                text_parts.append(c)
        except Exception:
            pass

    text = " ".join(text_parts).lower()

    if any(kw in text for kw in ["stange", "nut_d", "hydraulik"]):
        return "hydraulics_rod"
    return "rwdr"  # Default

def domain_router_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    try:
        domain = (detect_domain(state) or "rwdr").strip().lower()
        log.info("[domain_router] Detected domain: %s", domain)
        return {**state, "domain": domain, "phase": "domain_router"}
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[domain_router_node] Error: %s", e)
        return {**state, "domain": "rwdr", "phase": "domain_router", "error": str(e)}

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/domain_router.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/domain_router.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/domain_router.py
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional

from app.services.langgraph.graph.consult import utils as utils_mod

log = logging.getLogger("uvicorn.error")

def detect_domain(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[str]:
    """
    Heuristische Domain-Erkennung basierend auf params/messages im state.
    """
    params = state.get("params", {}) if state else {}
    msgs = utils_mod.normalize_messages(state.get("messages", [])) if state else []

    text_parts = []
    for v in params.values():
        if isinstance(v, str):
            text_parts.append(v)
    for m in msgs:
        try:
            c = getattr(m, "content", "") or ""
            if isinstance(c, str):
                text_parts.append(c)
        except Exception:
            pass

    text = " ".join(text_parts).lower()

    if any(kw in text for kw in ["stange", "nut_d", "hydraulik"]):
        return "hydraulics_rod"
    return "rwdr"  # Default

def domain_router_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    try:
        domain = (detect_domain(state) or "rwdr").strip().lower()
        log.info("[domain_router] Detected domain: %s", domain)
        return {**state, "domain": domain, "phase": "domain_router"}
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[domain_router_node] Error: %s", e)
        return {**state, "domain": "rwdr", "phase": "domain_router", "error": str(e)}

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/domain_router.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/domain_runtime.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/domain_runtime.py
from __future__ import annotations
import importlib
import logging
from typing import Any, Dict, List
from .state import Parameters, Derived

log = logging.getLogger(__name__)

def compute_domain(domain: str, params: Parameters) -> Derived:
    try:
        mod = importlib.import_module(f"app.services.langgraph.domains.{domain}.calculator")
        compute = getattr(mod, "compute")
        out = compute(params)  # type: ignore
        return {
            "calculated": dict(out.get("calculated", {})),
            "flags": dict(out.get("flags", {})),
            "warnings": list(out.get("warnings", [])),
            "requirements": list(out.get("requirements", [])),
        }
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning("Domain compute failed (%s): %s", domain, e)
        return {"calculated": {}, "flags": {}, "warnings": [], "requirements": []}

def missing_by_domain(domain: str, p: Parameters) -> List[str]:
    # ✅ Hydraulik-Stange nutzt stange_mm / nut_d_mm / nut_b_mm
    if domain == "hydraulics_rod":
        req = [
            "falltyp",
            "stange_mm",
            "nut_d_mm",
            "nut_b_mm",
            "medium",
            "temp_max_c",
            "druck_bar",
            "geschwindigkeit_m_s",
        ]
    else:
        req = [
            "falltyp",
            "wellen_mm",
            "gehause_mm",
            "breite_mm",
            "medium",
            "temp_max_c",
            "druck_bar",
            "drehzahl_u_min",
        ]

    def _is_missing(key: str, val: Any) -> bool:
        if val is None or val == "" or val == "unknown":
            return True
        if key == "druck_bar":
            try: float(val); return False
            except Exception: return True
        if key in ("wellen_mm", "gehause_mm", "breite_mm", "drehzahl_u_min", "geschwindigkeit_m_s",
                   "stange_mm", "nut_d_mm", "nut_b_mm"):
            try: return float(val) <= 0
            except Exception: return True
        if key == "temp_max_c":
            try: float(val); return False
            except Exception: return True
        return False

    return [k for k in req if _is_missing(k, p.get(k))]

def anomaly_messages(domain: str, params: Parameters, derived: Derived) -> List[str]:
    msgs: List[str] = []
    flags = (derived.get("flags") or {})
    if flags.get("requires_pressure_stage") and not flags.get("pressure_stage_ack"):
        msgs.append("Ein Überdruck >2 bar ist für Standard-Radialdichtringe kritisch. Dürfen Druckstufenlösungen geprüft werden?")
    if flags.get("speed_high"):
        msgs.append("Die Drehzahl/Umfangsgeschwindigkeit ist hoch – ist sie dauerhaft oder nur kurzzeitig (Spitzen)?")
    if flags.get("temp_very_high"):
        msgs.append("Die Temperatur ist sehr hoch. Handelt es sich um Dauer- oder Spitzentemperaturen?")
    if domain == "hydraulics_rod" and flags.get("extrusion_risk") and not flags.get("extrusion_risk_ack"):
        msgs.append("Bei dem Druck besteht Extrusionsrisiko. Darf eine Stütz-/Back-up-Ring-Lösung geprüft werden?")
    return msgs

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/domain_runtime.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/domain_runtime.py =====

from __future__ import annotations
import importlib
import logging
from typing import Any, Dict, List
from .state import Parameters, Derived

log = logging.getLogger(__name__)

def compute_domain(domain: str, params: Parameters) -> Derived:

        return {
            "calculated": dict(out.get("calculated", {})),
            "flags": dict(out.get("flags", {})),
            "warnings": list(out.get("warnings", [])),
            "requirements": list(out.get("requirements", [])),
        }
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning("Domain compute failed (%s): %s", domain, e)
        return {"calculated": {}, "flags": {}, "warnings": [], "requirements": []}

def missing_by_domain(domain: str, p: Parameters) -> List[str]:
    # ✅ Hydraulik-Stange nutzt stange_mm / nut_d_mm / nut_b_mm
    if domain == "hydraulics_rod":
        req = [
            "falltyp",
            "stange_mm",
            "nut_d_mm",
            "nut_b_mm",
            "medium",
            "temp_max_c",
            "druck_bar",
            "geschwindigkeit_m_s",
        ]
    else:
        req = [
            "falltyp",
            "wellen_mm",
            "gehause_mm",
            "breite_mm",
            "medium",
            "temp_max_c",
            "druck_bar",
            "drehzahl_u_min",
        ]

    def _is_missing(key: str, val: Any) -> bool:
        if val is None or val == "" or val == "unknown":
            return True
        if key == "druck_bar":
            try: float(val); return False
            except Exception: return True
        if key in ("wellen_mm", "gehause_mm", "breite_mm", "drehzahl_u_min", "geschwindigkeit_m_s",
                   "stange_mm", "nut_d_mm", "nut_b_mm"):
            try: return float(val) <= 0
            except Exception: return True
        if key == "temp_max_c":
            try: float(val); return False
            except Exception: return True
        return False

    return [k for k in req if _is_missing(k, p.get(k))]

def anomaly_messages(domain: str, params: Parameters, derived: Derived) -> List[str]:
    msgs: List[str] = []
    flags = (derived.get("flags") or {})
    if flags.get("requires_pressure_stage") and not flags.get("pressure_stage_ack"):
        msgs.append("Ein Überdruck >2 bar ist für Standard-Radialdichtringe kritisch. Dürfen Druckstufenlösungen geprüft werden?")
    if flags.get("speed_high"):
        msgs.append("Die Drehzahl/Umfangsgeschwindigkeit ist hoch – ist sie dauerhaft oder nur kurzzeitig (Spitzen)?")
    if flags.get("temp_very_high"):
        msgs.append("Die Temperatur ist sehr hoch. Handelt es sich um Dauer- oder Spitzentemperaturen?")
    if domain == "hydraulics_rod" and flags.get("extrusion_risk") and not flags.get("extrusion_risk_ack"):
        msgs.append("Bei dem Druck besteht Extrusionsrisiko. Darf eine Stütz-/Back-up-Ring-Lösung geprüft werden?")
    return msgs

===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/extract.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/extract.py
from __future__ import annotations

import json
import logging
import re
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

from langchain_core.messages import SystemMessage, HumanMessage
from app.services.langgraph.graph.consult.config import create_llm  # FIX: Nutzt fixierten LLM aus config
from app.services.langgraph.prompting import render_template

log = logging.getLogger(__name__)

# ============================================================
# einfache Heuristik als Fallback
# ============================================================

_NUMBER = r"[-+]?\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?"

def _to_float(x: Any) -> Optional[float]:
    try:
        if isinstance(x, (int, float)):
            return float(x)
        s = str(x).strip().replace(",", ".")
        return float(s)
    except Exception:
        return None

def heuristic_extract(user_input: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    txt = (user_input or "").lower()
    out: Dict[str, Any] = {"source": "heuristic"}

    if any(w in txt for w in ["rwdr", "wellendichtring", "radialwellendichtring"]):
        out["domain"] = "rwdr"; out["falltyp"] = "rwdr"
    elif any(w in txt for w in ["stangendichtung", "kolbenstange", "hydraulik"]):
        out["domain"] = "hydraulics_rod"; out["falltyp"] = "hydraulics_rod"

    m = re.search(rf"(?P<d>{_NUMBER})\s*[x×]\s*(?P<D>{_NUMBER})\s*[x×]\s*(?P<b>{_NUMBER})\s*mm", txt)
    if m:
        out["wellen_mm"]  = _to_float(m.group("d"))
        out["gehause_mm"] = _to_float(m.group("D"))
        out["breite_mm"]  = _to_float(m.group("b"))
    else:
        md = re.search(rf"(?:welle|d)\s*[:=]?\s*({_NUMBER})\s*mm", txt)
        mD = re.search(rf"(?:gehäuse|gehause|D)\s*[:=]?\s*({_NUMBER})\s*mm", txt)
        mb = re.search(rf"(?:breite|b)\s*[:=]?\s*({_NUMBER})\s*mm", txt)
        if md: out["wellen_mm"]  = _to_float(md.group(1))
        if mD: out["gehause_mm"] = _to_float(mD.group(1))
        if mb: out["breite_mm"]  = _to_float(mb.group(1))

    tmax = re.search(rf"(?:tmax|temp(?:eratur)?(?:\s*max)?)\s*[:=]?\s*({_NUMBER})\s*°?\s*c", txt)
    if not tmax:
        tmax = re.search(rf"({_NUMBER})\s*°?\s*c", txt)
    if tmax:
        out["temp_max_c"] = _to_float(tmax.group(1))

    p = re.search(rf"(?:p(?:_?max)?|druck)\s*[:=]?\s*({_NUMBER})\s*bar", txt)
    if p:
        out["druck_bar"] = _to_float(p.group(1))

    rpm = re.search(rf"(?:n|drehzahl|rpm)\s*[:=]?\s*({_NUMBER})\s*(?:u/?min|rpm)", txt)
    if rpm:
        out["drehzahl_u_min"] = _to_float(rpm.group(1))

    v = re.search(rf"(?:v|geschwindigkeit)\s*[:=]?\s*({_NUMBER})\s*m/?s", txt)
    if v:
        out["geschwindigkeit_m_s"] = _to_float(v.group(1))

    med = re.search(r"(?:medium|medien|stoff)\s*[:=]\s*([a-z0-9\-_/.,\s]+)", txt)
    if med:
        out["medium"] = med.group(1).strip()
    else:
        for k in ["öl", "oel", "diesel", "benzin", "kraftstoff", "wasser", "dampf", "säure", "saeure", "lauge"]:
            if k in txt:
                out["medium"] = k; break

    return out

# ============================================================
# robustes JSON aus LLM
# ============================================================

_JSON_RX = re.compile(r"\{[\s\S]*\}")

def _safe_json(text: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
    if not isinstance(text, str):
        return None
    try:
        return json.loads(text)
    except Exception:
        pass
    m = _JSON_RX.search(text)
    if not m:
        return None
    try:
        return json.loads(m.group(0))
    except Exception:
        return None

# ============================================================
# Öffentliche API (SIGNATUR passt zu build.py)
# ============================================================

def extract_params_with_llm(user_input: str, *, rag_context: str | None = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Extrahiert Pflicht-/Kernparameter aus der Nutzeranfrage.
    - FIX: korrektes Rendering von Jinja (keine zusätzlichen Positional-Args)
    - Normales Chat-Completion + robustes JSON-Parsing
    - Fallback: lokale Heuristik
    - Logging für Prompt/Response-Übertragung
    """
    try:
        sys_prompt = render_template(
            "consult_extract_params.jinja2",
            messages=[{"type": "user", "content": (user_input or "").strip()}],
            params_json="{}",
        )
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning("[extract_params_with_llm] template_render_failed: %r", e)
        return heuristic_extract(user_input)

    messages: List[Any] = [
        SystemMessage(content=sys_prompt),
        HumanMessage(content=user_input or ""),
    ]

    try:
        llm = create_llm(streaming=False, model="gpt-4o-mini")  # FIX: Echtes Runnable aus config
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning("[extract_params_with_llm] llm_factory_failed: %r", e)
        return heuristic_extract(user_input)

    try:
        resp = llm.invoke(messages)
        text = getattr(resp, "content", "") or ""
        log.info("[extract_params_with_llm] Prompt sent to LLM: %s | Response: %s", sys_prompt[:100] + "..." if len(sys_prompt) > 100 else sys_prompt, text[:100])  # FIX: Logging für Übertragung
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning("[extract_params_with_llm] llm_invoke_failed_plain: %r", e)
        return heuristic_extract(user_input)

    data = _safe_json(text)
    if not isinstance(data, dict):
        log.info("[extract_params_with_llm] no_json_in_response – using heuristic")
        return heuristic_extract(user_input)

    normalized: Dict[str, Any] = {}

    def _pick(name: str, *aliases: str, cast=None):
        for k in (name, *aliases):
            if k in data and data[k] is not None:
                v = data[k]
                if cast:
                    try:
                        v = cast(v)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                normalized[name] = v
                return

    _pick("falltyp")
    _pick("domain")
    _pick("wellen_mm", "stange_mm", cast=_to_float)
    _pick("gehause_mm", "nut_d_mm", cast=_to_float)
    _pick("breite_mm", "nut_b_mm", cast=_to_float)
    _pick("temp_max_c", cast=_to_float)
    _pick("drehzahl_u_min", cast=_to_float)
    _pick("druck_bar", cast=_to_float)
    _pick("geschwindigkeit_m_s", cast=_to_float)
    _pick("medium")

    for k, v in data.items():
        if k not in normalized:
            normalized[k] = v

    normalized.setdefault("source", "llm_json")
    return normalized

def extract_params(user_input: str, *, rag_context: str | None = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    return extract_params_with_llm(user_input, rag_context=rag_context)

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/extract.py =====

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/extract.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/heuristic_extract.py =====
from __future__ import annotations
import re
from typing import Dict, Optional

_NUM = r"-?\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?"

def _to_float(s: Optional[str]) -> Optional[float]:
    if not s:
        return None
    try:
        return float(s.replace(",", "."))
    except Exception:
        return None

def pre_extract_params(text: str) -> Dict[str, object]:
    t = text or ""
    out: Dict[str, object] = {}

    m = re.search(r"(?:\b(?:rwdr|ba|bauform)\b\s*)?(\d{1,3})\s*[x×]\s*(\d{1,3})\s*[x×]\s*(\d{1,3})", t, re.I)
    if m:
        out["wellen_mm"]  = int(m.group(1))
        out["gehause_mm"] = int(m.group(2))
        out["breite_mm"]  = int(m.group(3))

    if re.search(r"\bhydraulik ?öl\b", t, re.I):
        out["medium"] = "Hydrauliköl"
    elif re.search(r"\böl\b", t, re.I):
        out["medium"] = "Öl"
    elif re.search(r"\bwasser\b", t, re.I):
        out["medium"] = "Wasser"

    m = re.search(r"(?:t\s*max|temp(?:eratur)?(?:\s*max)?|t)\s*[:=]?\s*(" + _NUM + r")\s*°?\s*c\b", t, re.I)
    if not m:
        m = re.search(r"\b(" + _NUM + r")\s*°?\s*c\b", t, re.I)
    if m:
        out["temp_max_c"] = _to_float(m.group(1))

    m = re.search(r"(?:\bdruck\b|[^a-z]p)\s*[:=]?\s*(" + _NUM + r")\s*bar\b", t, re.I)
    if not m:
        m = re.search(r"\b(" + _NUM + r")\s*bar\b", t, re.I)
    if m:
        out["druck_bar"] = _to_float(m.group(1))

    m = re.search(r"(?:\bn\b|drehzahl)\s*[:=]?\s*(\d{1,7})\s*(?:u/?min|rpm)\b", t, re.I)
    if not m:
        m = re.search(r"\b(\d{1,7})\s*(?:u/?min|rpm)\b", t, re.I)
    if m:
        out["drehzahl_u_min"] = int(m.group(1))

    m = re.search(r"\bbauform\s*[:=]?\s*([A-Z0-9]{1,4})\b|\b(BA|B1|B2|TC|SC)\b", t, re.I)
    if m:
        out["bauform"] = (m.group(1) or m.group(2) or "").upper()

    return out

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/heuristic_extract.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/heuristic_extract.py =====
from __future__ import annotations
import re
from typing import Dict, Optional

_NUM = r"-?\d+(?:[.,]\d+)?"

def _to_float(s: Optional[str]) -> Optional[float]:
    if not s:
        return None
    try:
        return float(s.replace(",", "."))
    except Exception:
        return None

def pre_extract_params(text: str) -> Dict[str, object]:
    t = text or ""
    out: Dict[str, object] = {}

    m = re.search(r"(?:\b(?:rwdr|ba|bauform)\b\s*)?(\d{1,3})\s*[x×]\s*(\d{1,3})\s*[x×]\s*(\d{1,3})", t, re.I)
    if m:
        out["wellen_mm"]  = int(m.group(1))
        out["gehause_mm"] = int(m.group(2))
        out["breite_mm"]  = int(m.group(3))

    if re.search(r"\bhydraulik ?öl\b", t, re.I):
        out["medium"] = "Hydrauliköl"
    elif re.search(r"\böl\b", t, re.I):
        out["medium"] = "Öl"
    elif re.search(r"\bwasser\b", t, re.I):
        out["medium"] = "Wasser"

    m = re.search(r"(?:t\s*max|temp(?:eratur)?(?:\s*max)?|t)\s*[:=]?\s*(" + _NUM + r")\s*°?\s*c\b", t, re.I)
    if not m:
        m = re.search(r"\b(" + _NUM + r")\s*°?\s*c\b", t, re.I)
    if m:
        out["temp_max_c"] = _to_float(m.group(1))

    m = re.search(r"(?:\bdruck\b|[^a-z]p)\s*[:=]?\s*(" + _NUM + r")\s*bar\b", t, re.I)
    if not m:
        m = re.search(r"\b(" + _NUM + r")\s*bar\b", t, re.I)
    if m:
        out["druck_bar"] = _to_float(m.group(1))

    m = re.search(r"(?:\bn\b|drehzahl)\s*[:=]?\s*(\d{1,7})\s*(?:u/?min|rpm)\b", t, re.I)
    if not m:
        m = re.search(r"\b(\d{1,7})\s*(?:u/?min|rpm)\b", t, re.I)
    if m:
        out["drehzahl_u_min"] = int(m.group(1))

    m = re.search(r"\bbauform\s*[:=]?\s*([A-Z0-9]{1,4})\b|\b(BA|B1|B2|TC|SC)\b", t, re.I)
    if m:
        out["bauform"] = (m.group(1) or m.group(2) or "").upper()

    return out

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/heuristic_extract.py =====

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/__init__.py =====

===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/io.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/io.py
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from typing import Any, Optional
from langchain_core.messages import AIMessage, HumanMessage

from .build import build_graph as build_consult_graph
from .config import RECURSION_LIMIT
from .state import ConsultState
from . import utils as utils_mod
from langgraph.checkpoint.memory import MemorySaver  # Primary Fallback für async

try:
    from app.services.langgraph.redis_lifespan import get_redis_checkpointer
    REDIS_AVAILABLE = True
except ImportError:
    REDIS_AVAILABLE = False
    get_redis_checkpointer = None  # type: ignore

log = logging.getLogger("uvicorn.error")


async def invoke_consult(text: str, thread_id: str, checkpointer: Optional[Any] = None) -> str:
    """
    Invoke the ConsultGraph: Fügt User-Input als Message hinzu, läuft Graph, extrahiert finalen AI-Text.

    Design:
    - Für asynchrone Aufrufe nutzen wir standardmäßig MemorySaver (stabil).
    - Wenn explizit ein Checkpointer übergeben wird, verwenden wir ihn nur,
      wenn er async-Methoden (aget_tuple) unterstützt.
    - Zusätzlich setzen wir ein defensives recursion_limit, um Endlosschleifen zu verhindern.
    """
    try:
        # --- Checkpointer-Strategie (async-sicher) ---
        cp = None
        if checkpointer is not None:
            # Nur verwenden, wenn async unterstützt ist
            if hasattr(checkpointer, "aget_tuple") and callable(getattr(checkpointer, "aget_tuple")):
                cp = checkpointer
            else:
                log.warning("[invoke_consult] Übergebener Checkpointer ohne async-Unterstützung – falle auf MemorySaver zurück.")
                cp = MemorySaver()
        else:
            # Optional: Redis laden, aber nur wenn async unterstützt
            if REDIS_AVAILABLE and get_redis_checkpointer is not None:
                try:
                    redis_cp = get_redis_checkpointer()
                    if redis_cp and hasattr(redis_cp, "aget_tuple") and callable(getattr(redis_cp, "aget_tuple")):
                        cp = redis_cp
                        log.info("[invoke_consult] Using RedisSaver (async-ready) checkpointer")
                    else:
                        cp = MemorySaver()
                        if redis_cp is not None:
                            log.warning("[invoke_consult] RedisSaver ohne async-Unterstützung – MemorySaver aktiv.")
                except Exception as e:
                    log.warning("[invoke_consult] Redis checkpointer fehlgeschlagen (%s) – MemorySaver aktiv.", e)
                    cp = MemorySaver()
            else:
                cp = MemorySaver()

        log.info(
            "[invoke_consult] Starting with text='%s', thread_id='%s', checkpointer=%s",
            text[:50] + "..." if len(text) > 50 else text,
            thread_id,
            type(cp).__name__,
        )

        # Graph bauen
        graph = build_consult_graph(checkpointer=cp)

        # Frischer Initialzustand
        initial_state: ConsultState = {
            "messages": [HumanMessage(content=text)],
            "params": {},
            "thread_id": thread_id,
            "phase": "init",
            "metrics": {},
        }

        # Graph ausführen (asynchron) – mit Sicherheitsleine
        final_state = await graph.ainvoke(
            initial_state,
            config={
                "configurable": {"thread_id": thread_id},
                "recursion_limit": RECURSION_LIMIT,
            },
        )

        log.info("[invoke_consult] Final phase: %s", final_state.get("phase", "unknown"))

        # Finalen AI-Text extrahieren (letzte AI-Message)
        messages = utils_mod.normalize_messages(final_state.get("messages", []))
        if messages:
            last_msg = messages[-1]
            if isinstance(last_msg, AIMessage):
                output_text = last_msg.content or "No response generated."
                log.info(
                    "[invoke_consult] Extracted output: %s",
                    output_text[:100] + "..." if len(output_text) > 100 else output_text,
                )
                return output_text
            else:
                log.warning("[invoke_consult] Last message not AI: %s", type(last_msg))

        # Fallback: Wenn kein AI-Message, nimm aus "answer" oder "explanation"
        fallback = final_state.get("answer") or final_state.get("explanation") or "Graph completed without response."
        log.warning("[invoke_consult] Fallback to state field: %s", (fallback or "")[:50])
        return fallback

    except NotImplementedError as e:
        # Typischer Fall: Checkpointer hat keine async-Methoden
        if "aget_tuple" in str(e) or "checkpointer" in str(e):
            log.warning("[invoke_consult] Checkpointer async error (%s), retrying with MemorySaver", e)
            return await invoke_consult(text, thread_id, MemorySaver())
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[invoke_consult] Error during graph invoke: %s", e, exc_info=True)
        return f"Fehler beim Verarbeiten: {str(e)}"  # User-freundlicher Fallback


# Sync-Wrapper für non-async Calls (z.B. Warmup)
def invoke_consult_sync(text: str, thread_id: str, checkpointer: Optional[Any] = None) -> str:
    import asyncio
    return asyncio.run(invoke_consult(text, thread_id, checkpointer))

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/io.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/io.py =====

import logging
from typing import Any, Optional
from langchain_core.messages import AIMessage, HumanMessage

from .build import build_graph as build_consult_graph

===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/memory_utils.py =====
from __future__ import annotations

import os
import json
from typing import List, Dict, Literal, TypedDict

from redis import Redis
from langchain_core.messages import HumanMessage, AIMessage, SystemMessage, AnyMessage


def _redis() -> Redis:
    url = os.getenv("REDIS_URL", "redis://redis:6379/0")
    return Redis.from_url(url, decode_responses=True)

def _conv_key(thread_id: str) -> str:
    # Gleicher Key wie im SSE: chat:stm:{thread_id}:messages
    return f"chat:stm:{thread_id}:messages"

def _summary_key(thread_id: str) -> str:
    return f"chat:stm:{thread_id}:summary"


def _last_agent_key(thread_id: str) -> str:
    return f"chat:stm:{thread_id}:last_agent"


def write_message(*, thread_id: str, role: Literal["user", "assistant", "system"], content: str) -> None:
    if not content:
        return
    r = _redis()
    key = _conv_key(thread_id)
    item = json.dumps({"role": role, "content": content}, ensure_ascii=False)
    pipe = r.pipeline()
    pipe.lpush(key, item)
    pipe.ltrim(key, 0, int(os.getenv("STM_MAX_ITEMS", "200")) - 1)
    pipe.expire(key, int(os.getenv("STM_TTL_SEC", "604800")))  # 7 Tage
    pipe.execute()


def set_summary(thread_id: str, content: str) -> None:
    """Persistiert eine kompakte Thread-Zusammenfassung separat, mit derselben TTL wie STM."""
    if not content:
        return
    r = _redis()
    key = _summary_key(thread_id)
    r.set(key, content)
    r.expire(key, int(os.getenv("STM_TTL_SEC", "604800")))


def set_last_agent(thread_id: str, agent: str) -> None:
    if not agent:
        return
    r = _redis()
    key = _last_agent_key(thread_id)
    ttl = int(os.getenv("STM_TTL_SEC", "604800"))
    try:
        r.set(key, agent)
        r.expire(key, ttl)
    except Exception:
        pass


def get_last_agent(thread_id: str) -> str | None:
    r = _redis()
    key = _last_agent_key(thread_id)
    try:
        raw = r.get(key)
    except Exception:
        return None
    if isinstance(raw, str) and raw.strip():
        return raw.strip()
    return None


def read_history_raw(thread_id: str, limit: int = 80) -> List[Dict[str, str]]:
    """Rohdaten (älteste -> neueste)."""
    r = _redis()
    key = _conv_key(thread_id)
    items = r.lrange(key, 0, limit - 1) or []
    # Optional vorgespeicherte Summary als erste Systemnachricht einfügen
    summary_txt = r.get(_summary_key(thread_id))
    out: List[Dict[str, str]] = []
    if isinstance(summary_txt, str) and summary_txt.strip():
        out.append({"role": "system", "content": summary_txt.strip()})
    for s in reversed(items):  # Redis speichert neueste zuerst
        try:
            obj = json.loads(s)
            role = (obj.get("role") or "").lower()
            content = obj.get("content") or ""
            if role and content:
                out.append({"role": role, "content": content})
        except Exception:
            continue
    return out


def read_history(thread_id: str, limit: int = 80) -> List[AnyMessage]:
    """LangChain-Messages (älteste -> neueste)."""
    msgs: List[AnyMessage] = []
    for item in read_history_raw(thread_id, limit=limit):
        role = item["role"]
        content = item["content"]
        if role in ("user", "human"):
            msgs.append(HumanMessage(content=content))
        elif role in ("assistant", "ai"):
            msgs.append(AIMessage(content=content))
        elif role == "system":
            msgs.append(SystemMessage(content=content))
    return msgs

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/memory_utils.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/memory_utils.py =====

            msgs.append(AIMessage(content=content))
        elif role == "system":
            msgs.append(SystemMessage(content=content))
    return msgs

===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/ask_missing.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/ask_missing.py
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from typing import Any, Dict, List

from langchain_core.messages import HumanMessage, AIMessage

from app.services.langgraph.prompting import render_template, messages_for_template
from ..config import create_llm  # nutzt denselben LLM-Factory-Path wie intent_llm

log = logging.getLogger("uvicorn.error")

# Pflichtfelder je Domain zentral
MISSING_BY_DOMAIN: Dict[str, List[str]] = {
    "rwdr": [
        "falltyp", "wellen_mm", "gehause_mm", "breite_mm",
        "medium", "temp_max_c", "druck_bar", "drehzahl_u_min"
    ],
    "hydraulics_rod": [
        "druck_bar", "medium", "temp_max_c", "hub_mm", "geschwindigkeit_mm_s"
    ],
    "generic": [
        "medium", "temp_max_c", "druck_bar"
    ],
}

def missing_by_domain(domain: str, params: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[str]:
    required = MISSING_BY_DOMAIN.get(domain, MISSING_BY_DOMAIN["generic"])
    miss: List[str] = []
    for k in required:
        v = params.get(k)
        if v is None:
            miss.append(k); continue
        if isinstance(v, str) and not v.strip():
            miss.append(k); continue
        if isinstance(v, (list, dict)) and not v:
            miss.append(k); continue
        if isinstance(v, str) and v.strip().lower() == "unknown":
            miss.append(k); continue
    return miss


def ask_missing_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Erzeugt eine fokussierte Rückfrage an den Nutzer, wenn Pflichtfelder fehlen.
    Fügt die Frage als AI-Message in state['messages'] an.
    """
    try:
        params = state.get("params", {}) or {}
        domain = (state.get("domain") or params.get("domain") or "rwdr").strip().lower()
        # ✅ robustes Default für Sprache – verhindert 'lang is undefined'
        lang = (state.get("lang") or params.get("lang") or "de").strip().lower()

        missing = missing_by_domain(domain, params)

        # Falls nichts fehlt, nur Phase markieren – Routing übernimmt _ask_or_ok in build.py
        if not missing:
            return {**state, "phase": "ask_missing"}

        prompt = render_template(
            "ask_missing_llm_user.jinja2",
            domain=domain,
            missing=missing,
            params=params,
            lang=lang,  # ✅ explizit übergeben
            messages=messages_for_template(state.get("messages", [])),
        )
        log.info("[ask_missing] Prompt sent to LLM: %s", (prompt[:200] + "...") if len(prompt) > 200 else prompt)

        llm = create_llm(streaming=False)
        resp = llm.invoke([HumanMessage(content=prompt)])
        content = (getattr(resp, "content", "") or "").strip()
        if not content:
            content = f"Um fortzufahren, brauche ich noch folgende Angaben ({domain}): {', '.join(missing)}."

        log.info("[ask_missing] LLM response: %s", (content[:200] + "...") if len(content) > 200 else content)

        assistant_msg = AIMessage(content=content)
        new_state = dict(state)
        new_state["messages"] = new_state.get("messages", []) + [assistant_msg]
        new_state["phase"] = "ask_missing"
        return new_state

    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[ask_missing_node] Error: %s", e)
        fallback_msg = AIMessage(
            content="Um eine Empfehlung zu geben, brauche ich mehr Details zu Maßen, Medium, Temperatur etc. – öffne das Formular!"
        )
        return {**state, "messages": state.get("messages", []) + [fallback_msg], "phase": "ask_missing"}

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/ask_missing.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/ask_missing.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/ask_missing.py
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from typing import Any, Dict, List

from langchain_core.messages import HumanMessage, AIMessage

from app.services.langgraph.prompting import render_template, messages_for_template
from ..config import create_llm  # nutzt denselben LLM-Factory-Path wie intent_llm

log = logging.getLogger("uvicorn.error")

# Pflichtfelder je Domain zentral
MISSING_BY_DOMAIN: Dict[str, List[str]] = {
    "rwdr": [
        "falltyp", "wellen_mm", "gehause_mm", "breite_mm",
        "medium", "temp_max_c", "druck_bar", "drehzahl_u_min"
    ],
    "hydraulics_rod": [
        "druck_bar", "medium", "temp_max_c", "hub_mm", "geschwindigkeit_mm_s"
    ],
    "generic": [
        "medium", "temp_max_c", "druck_bar"
    ],
}

def missing_by_domain(domain: str, params: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[str]:
    required = MISSING_BY_DOMAIN.get(domain, MISSING_BY_DOMAIN["generic"])
    miss: List[str] = []
    for k in required:
        v = params.get(k)
        if v is None:
            miss.append(k); continue
        if isinstance(v, str) and not v.strip():
            miss.append(k); continue
        if isinstance(v, (list, dict)) and not v:
            miss.append(k); continue
        if isinstance(v, str) and v.strip().lower() == "unknown":
            miss.append(k); continue
    return miss


def ask_missing_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Erzeugt eine fokussierte Rückfrage an den Nutzer, wenn Pflichtfelder fehlen.
    Fügt die Frage als AI-Message in state['messages'] an.
    """
    try:
        params = state.get("params", {}) or {}
        domain = (state.get("domain") or params.get("domain") or "rwdr").strip().lower()
        # ✅ robustes Default für Sprache – verhindert 'lang is undefined'
        lang = (state.get("lang") or params.get("lang") or "de").strip().lower()

        missing = missing_by_domain(domain, params)

        # Falls nichts fehlt, nur Phase markieren – Routing übernimmt _ask_or_ok in build.py
        if not missing:
            return {**state, "phase": "ask_missing"}

        prompt = render_template(
            "ask_missing_llm_user.jinja2",
            domain=domain,
            missing=missing,
            params=params,
            lang=lang,  # ✅ explizit übergeben
            messages=messages_for_template(state.get("messages", [])),
        )
        log.info("[ask_missing] Prompt sent to LLM: %s", (prompt[:200] + "...") if len(prompt) > 200 else prompt)

        llm = create_llm(streaming=False)
        resp = llm.invoke([HumanMessage(content=prompt)])
        content = (getattr(resp, "content", "") or "").strip()
        if not content:
            content = f"Um fortzufahren, brauche ich noch folgende Angaben ({domain}): {', '.join(missing)}."

        log.info("[ask_missing] LLM response: %s", (content[:200] + "...") if len(content) > 200 else content)

        assistant_msg = AIMessage(content=content)
        new_state = dict(state)
        new_state["messages"] = new_state.get("messages", []) + [assistant_msg]
        new_state["phase"] = "ask_missing"
        return new_state

    except Exception as e:

        fallback_msg = AIMessage(
            content="Um eine Empfehlung zu geben, brauche ich mehr Details zu Maßen, Medium, Temperatur etc. – öffne das Formular!"

===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/calc_agent.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/calc_agent.py
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from typing import Any, Dict

log = logging.getLogger(__name__)

def _num(x: Any) -> float | None:
    try:
        if x in (None, "", []):
            return None
        if isinstance(x, bool):
            return None
        return float(x)
    except Exception:
        return None

def _deep_merge(a: Dict[str, Any], b: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    out = dict(a or {})
    for k, v in (b or {}).items():
        if isinstance(v, dict) and isinstance(out.get(k), dict):
            out[k] = _deep_merge(out[k], v)
        else:
            out[k] = v
    return out

def _calc_rwdr(params: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    d_mm = _num(params.get("wellen_mm"))
    n_rpm = _num(params.get("drehzahl_u_min"))
    p_bar = _num(params.get("druck_bar"))
    tmax = _num(params.get("temp_max_c"))

    calc: Dict[str, Any] = {}
    if d_mm is not None and n_rpm is not None and d_mm > 0 and n_rpm >= 0:
        d_m = d_mm / 1000.0
        v_ms = 3.141592653589793 * d_m * (n_rpm / 60.0)
        calc["umfangsgeschwindigkeit_m_s"] = v_ms
        calc["surface_speed_m_s"] = round(v_ms, 3)

    if p_bar is not None and calc.get("umfangsgeschwindigkeit_m_s") is not None:
        calc["pv_indicator_bar_ms"] = p_bar * calc["umfangsgeschwindigkeit_m_s"]

    mat_whitelist: list[str] = []
    mat_blacklist: list[str] = []
    medium = (params.get("medium") or "").strip().lower()
    # KEINE harte PTFE-Blacklist bei Wasser
    if "wasser" in medium:
        mat_whitelist.extend(["EPDM", "FKM", "PTFE"])

    if tmax is not None:
        if tmax > 120:
            mat_whitelist.append("FKM")
        if tmax > 200:
            mat_whitelist.append("PTFE")

    reqs: list[str] = []
    flags: Dict[str, Any] = {}
    if p_bar is not None and p_bar > 1.0:
        flags["druckbelastet"] = True

    return {
        "calculated": calc,
        "material_whitelist": mat_whitelist,
        "material_blacklist": mat_blacklist,
        "requirements": reqs,
        "flags": flags,
    }

def _calc_hydraulics_rod(params: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    p_bar = _num(params.get("druck_bar"))
    v_lin = _num(params.get("geschwindigkeit_m_s"))
    tmax = _num(params.get("temp_max_c"))

    calc: Dict[str, Any] = {}
    if p_bar is not None and v_lin is not None:
        calc["pv_indicator_bar_ms"] = p_bar * v_lin

    flags: Dict[str, Any] = {}
    reqs: list[str] = []
    if p_bar is not None and p_bar >= 160:
        flags["extrusion_risk"] = True
        reqs.append("Stütz-/Back-up-Ring prüfen (≥160 bar).")

    mat_whitelist: list[str] = []
    if tmax is not None and tmax > 100:
        mat_whitelist.append("FKM")

    return {
        "calculated": calc,
        "flags": flags,
        "requirements": reqs,
        "material_whitelist": mat_whitelist,
        "material_blacklist": [],
    }

def calc_agent_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Domänenspezifische Heuristiken ergänzen und mit derived mergen.
    Sendet ebenfalls einen calc_snapshot fürs UI.
    """
    domain = (state.get("domain") or "rwdr").strip().lower()
    params = dict(state.get("params") or {})
    derived_existing = dict(state.get("derived") or {})

    try:
        if domain == "hydraulics_rod":
            derived_new = _calc_hydraulics_rod(params)
        else:
            derived_new = _calc_rwdr(params)
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning("[calc_agent] calc_failed", exc=str(e))
        return {**state, "phase": "calc_agent"}

    derived_merged = _deep_merge(derived_existing, derived_new)

    v = (
        derived_merged.get("calculated", {}).get("umfangsgeschwindigkeit_m_s")
        or params.get("relativgeschwindigkeit_ms")
    )
    if v is not None:
        derived_merged["relativgeschwindigkeit_ms"] = v

    new_state = {**state, "derived": derived_merged, "phase": "calc_agent"}
    new_state["ui_event"] = {"ui_action": "calc_snapshot", "derived": derived_merged}
    return new_state

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/calc_agent.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/calc_agent.py =====

import logging
from typing import Any, Dict

log = logging.getLogger(__name__)

def _num(x: Any) -> float | None:
    try:
        if x in (None, "", []):
            return None
        if isinstance(x, bool):
            return None
        return float(x)

        return None

        if isinstance(v, dict) and isinstance(out.get(k), dict):
            out[k] = _deep_merge(out[k], v)
        else:
            out[k] = v
    return out

        "requirements": reqs,
        "material_whitelist": mat_whitelist,
        "material_blacklist": [],
    }

def calc_agent_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Domänenspezifische Heuristiken ergänzen und mit derived mergen.

# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/critique.py
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
import re  # FIX: Für Score-Parsing hinzugefügt
from typing import Any, Dict

from langchain_core.messages import HumanMessage, AIMessage

# FIX: Absolute Imports für Robustheit (basierend auf Tree-Struktur)
from app.services.langgraph.prompting import render_template, messages_for_template
from app.services.langgraph.graph.consult.config import create_llm

log = logging.getLogger("uvicorn.error")

def critique_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Self-Critique-Node: Validiert Annahmen in der aktuellen Empfehlung/Erklärung.
    - Prompt: LLM bewertet Evidenz, Bias und Unsicherheiten (Score 0-1).
    - Setzt 'critique_score' für _critique_key.
    - Passt zu Konzept: Reflexionsloop für Stability.
    """
    try:
        # Aktueller Kontext (z.B. aus recommend/explain)
        recommendation = state.get("answer", "") or state.get("explanation", "")
        params = state.get("params", {})
        domain = state.get("domain", "rwdr")
        messages = state.get("messages", [])

        # Render Prompt (erweitere prompts/ um critique.jinja2, falls nicht vorhanden)
        prompt = render_template(
            "critique.jinja2",  # TODO: Erstelle prompts/critique.jinja2 mit: "Valide diese Empfehlung: {{recommendation}}. Params: {{params}}. Score 0-1 für Evidenz und Bias-Freiheit."
            recommendation=recommendation,
            params=params,
            domain=domain,
            messages=messages_for_template(messages),
        )

        llm = create_llm(streaming=False, model="gpt-4o-mini")  # Leichtes Modell
        resp = llm.invoke([HumanMessage(content=prompt)])
        content = getattr(resp, "content", "").strip()

        # Parse Score (einfach: suche nach "Score: X" oder fallback)
        score_match = re.search(r'score[:\s]*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)', content, re.IGNORECASE)
        critique_score = float(score_match.group(1)) if score_match else 0.5  # Fallback 0.5
        critique_reason = content  # Für Logging/UI

        log.info("[critique_node] Score: %.2f for domain=%s", critique_score, domain)

        # Assistant-Message mit Feedback
        assistant_msg = AIMessage(
            content=f"Critique: {critique_reason[:200]}... (Score: {critique_score:.2f})"
        )

        new_state = dict(state)
        new_state["critique_score"] = critique_score
        new_state["critique_reason"] = critique_reason

        return {
            **new_state,
            "messages": new_state.get("messages", []) + [assistant_msg],
            "phase": "critique",
        }
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[critique_node] Error: %s", e)
        # Recovery: Neutraler Score, route zu safety
        return {
            **state,
            "critique_score": 0.8,  # "OK" Threshold
            "critique_reason": "Critique skipped due to error.",
            "phase": "critique",
        }

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/critique.py =====

===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/deterministic_calc.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/deterministic_calc.py
from __future__ import annotations

import math
from typing import Any, Dict

def _to_float(x, default=None):
    try:
        if x is None or x == "" or x == "unknown":
            return default
        if isinstance(x, (int, float)):
            return float(x)
        s = str(x).replace(" ", "").replace(",", ".")
        return float(s)
    except Exception:
        return default

def _max_defined(*vals):
    for v in vals:
        if v is not None:
            return v
    return None

def deterministic_calc_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Deterministische Kernberechnungen (kein LLM):
      - v, ω, p (bar/Pa/MPa), PV (bar·m/s / MPa·m/s)
      - optional Reibkraft & Reibleistung (falls Parameter vorhanden)
    Ergänzt state['derived'] nicht-destruktiv und sendet ein UI-Snapshot-Event.
    """
    params: Dict[str, Any] = dict(state.get("params") or {})
    derived: Dict[str, Any] = dict(state.get("derived") or {})

    d_mm   = _max_defined(_to_float(params.get("wellen_mm")), _to_float(params.get("stange_mm")))
    rpm    = _max_defined(_to_float(params.get("drehzahl_u_min")), _to_float(params.get("n_u_min")), _to_float(params.get("rpm")))
    v_ms   = _max_defined(_to_float(params.get("relativgeschwindigkeit_ms")), _to_float(params.get("geschwindigkeit_m_s")), _to_float(params.get("v_ms")))
    p_bar  = _max_defined(_to_float(params.get("druck_bar")), _to_float(params.get("pressure_bar")))
    width_mm = _to_float(params.get("width_mm"))
    mu     = _to_float(params.get("mu"))
    p_contact_mpa = _to_float(params.get("contact_pressure_mpa"))
    axial_force_n = _to_float(params.get("axial_force_n"))

    # v
    if v_ms is None and d_mm is not None and rpm is not None and d_mm > 0 and rpm > 0:
        v_ms = math.pi * (d_mm / 1000.0) * (rpm / 60.0)

    # ω
    omega = 2.0 * math.pi * (rpm / 60.0) if rpm is not None else None

    # p
    p_pa = p_mpa = None
    if p_bar is not None:
        p_pa = p_bar * 1e5
        p_mpa = p_bar / 10.0

    # PV
    pv_bar_ms = pv_mpa_ms = None
    if p_bar is not None and v_ms is not None:
        pv_bar_ms = p_bar * v_ms
        pv_mpa_ms = (p_bar / 10.0) * v_ms

    # Reibung/Leistung (Variante A: über Axialkraft)
    friction_force_n = friction_power_w = None
    if axial_force_n is not None and mu is not None and v_ms is not None:
        friction_force_n = mu * axial_force_n
        friction_power_w = friction_force_n * v_ms
    # Variante B: Kontaktpressung * Fläche
    elif (p_contact_mpa is not None) and (d_mm is not None) and (width_mm is not None) and (mu is not None) and (v_ms is not None):
        d_m = d_mm / 1000.0
        b_m = width_mm / 1000.0
        area_m2 = math.pi * d_m * b_m
        normal_force_n = (p_contact_mpa * 1e6) * area_m2
        friction_force_n = mu * normal_force_n
        friction_power_w = friction_force_n * v_ms

    # write back
    calc = dict(derived.get("calculated") or {})
    if v_ms is not None:
        calc["umfangsgeschwindigkeit_m_s"] = round(v_ms, 6)
        calc["surface_speed_m_s"] = round(v_ms, 6)
    if omega is not None:
        calc["omega_rad_s"] = round(omega, 6)
    if p_bar is not None:
        calc["p_bar"] = round(p_bar, 6)
    if p_pa is not None:
        calc["p_pa"] = round(p_pa, 3)
    if p_mpa is not None:
        calc["p_mpa"] = round(p_mpa, 6)
    if pv_bar_ms is not None:
        calc["pv_bar_ms"] = round(pv_bar_ms, 6)
    if pv_mpa_ms is not None:
        calc["pv_mpa_ms"] = round(pv_mpa_ms, 6)
    if friction_force_n is not None:
        calc["friction_force_n"] = round(friction_force_n, 6)
    if friction_power_w is not None:
        calc["friction_power_w"] = round(friction_power_w, 6)

    flags = dict(derived.get("flags") or {})
    warnings = list(derived.get("warnings") or [])
    if pv_mpa_ms is not None and pv_mpa_ms > 0.5:
        warnings.append(f"PV-Kennzahl hoch ({pv_mpa_ms:.3f} MPa·m/s) – Material/Profil prüfen.")

    new_derived = dict(derived)
    new_derived["calculated"] = calc
    new_derived["flags"] = flags
    new_derived["warnings"] = warnings

    # UI-Snapshot für Sidebar
    ui_event = {"ui_action": "calc_snapshot", "derived": new_derived}

    # Kompatibilitätsalias
    if v_ms is not None:
        new_derived["relativgeschwindigkeit_ms"] = v_ms

    return {**state, "derived": new_derived, "phase": "deterministic_calc", "ui_event": ui_event}

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/deterministic_calc.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/deterministic_calc.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/deterministic_calc.py
from __future__ import annotations

import math
from typing import Any, Dict

def _to_float(x, default=None):
    try:
        if x is None or x == "" or x == "unknown":
            return default
        if isinstance(x, (int, float)):
            return float(x)
        s = str(x).replace(" ", "").replace(",", ".")
        return float(s)
    except Exception:
        return default

def _max_defined(*vals):
    for v in vals:
        if v is not None:
            return v
    return None

def deterministic_calc_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Deterministische Kernberechnungen (kein LLM):
      - v, ω, p (bar/Pa/MPa), PV (bar·m/s / MPa·m/s)
      - optional Reibkraft & Reibleistung (falls Parameter vorhanden)
    Ergänzt state['derived'] nicht-destruktiv und sendet ein UI-Snapshot-Event.
    """
    params: Dict[str, Any] = dict(state.get("params") or {})
    derived: Dict[str, Any] = dict(state.get("derived") or {})

    d_mm   = _max_defined(_to_float(params.get("wellen_mm")), _to_float(params.get("stange_mm")))
    rpm    = _max_defined(_to_float(params.get("drehzahl_u_min")), _to_float(params.get("n_u_min")), _to_float(params.get("rpm")))
    v_ms   = _max_defined(_to_float(params.get("relativgeschwindigkeit_ms")), _to_float(params.get("geschwindigkeit_m_s")), _to_float(params.get("v_ms")))
    p_bar  = _max_defined(_to_float(params.get("druck_bar")), _to_float(params.get("pressure_bar")))
    width_mm = _to_float(params.get("width_mm"))
    mu     = _to_float(params.get("mu"))
    p_contact_mpa = _to_float(params.get("contact_pressure_mpa"))
    axial_force_n = _to_float(params.get("axial_force_n"))

    # v
    if v_ms is None and d_mm is not None and rpm is not None and d_mm > 0 and rpm > 0:
        v_ms = math.pi * (d_mm / 1000.0) * (rpm / 60.0)

    # ω
    omega = 2.0 * math.pi * (rpm / 60.0) if rpm is not None else None

    # p
    p_pa = p_mpa = None
    if p_bar is not None:
        p_pa = p_bar * 1e5
        p_mpa = p_bar / 10.0

    # PV
    pv_bar_ms = pv_mpa_ms = None
    if p_bar is not None and v_ms is not None:
        pv_bar_ms = p_bar * v_ms
        pv_mpa_ms = (p_bar / 10.0) * v_ms

    # Reibung/Leistung (Variante A: über Axialkraft)
    friction_force_n = friction_power_w = None
    if axial_force_n is not None and mu is not None and v_ms is not None:
        friction_force_n = mu * axial_force_n
        friction_power_w = friction_force_n * v_ms
    # Variante B: Kontaktpressung * Fläche
    elif (p_contact_mpa is not None) and (d_mm is not None) and (width_mm is not None) and (mu is not None) and (v_ms is not None):
        d_m = d_mm / 1000.0
        b_m = width_mm / 1000.0
        area_m2 = math.pi * d_m * b_m
        normal_force_n = (p_contact_mpa * 1e6) * area_m2
        friction_force_n = mu * normal_force_n
        friction_power_w = friction_force_n * v_ms

    # write back
    calc = dict(derived.get("calculated") or {})
    if v_ms is not None:
        calc["umfangsgeschwindigkeit_m_s"] = round(v_ms, 6)
        calc["surface_speed_m_s"] = round(v_ms, 6)
    if omega is not None:
        calc["omega_rad_s"] = round(omega, 6)
    if p_bar is not None:
        calc["p_bar"] = round(p_bar, 6)
    if p_pa is not None:
        calc["p_pa"] = round(p_pa, 3)
    if p_mpa is not None:
        calc["p_mpa"] = round(p_mpa, 6)
    if pv_bar_ms is not None:
        calc["pv_bar_ms"] = round(pv_bar_ms, 6)
    if pv_mpa_ms is not None:
        calc["pv_mpa_ms"] = round(pv_mpa_ms, 6)
    if friction_force_n is not None:
        calc["friction_force_n"] = round(friction_force_n, 6)
    if friction_power_w is not None:
        calc["friction_power_w"] = round(friction_power_w, 6)

    flags = dict(derived.get("flags") or {})
    warnings = list(derived.get("warnings") or [])
    if pv_mpa_ms is not None and pv_mpa_ms > 0.5:
        warnings.append(f"PV-Kennzahl hoch ({pv_mpa_ms:.3f} MPa·m/s) – Material/Profil prüfen.")

    new_derived = dict(derived)
    new_derived["calculated"] = calc
    new_derived["flags"] = flags
    new_derived["warnings"] = warnings

    # UI-Snapshot für Sidebar
    ui_event = {"ui_action": "calc_snapshot", "derived": new_derived}

    # Kompatibilitätsalias
    if v_ms is not None:
        new_derived["relativgeschwindigkeit_ms"] = v_ms

    return {**state, "derived": new_derived, "phase": "deterministic_calc", "ui_event": ui_event}

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/deterministic_calc.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/explain.py =====
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
import json
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Tuple

from langchain_core.messages import AIMessage

log = logging.getLogger(__name__)

def _hashable_key(obj: Any) -> Any:
    if isinstance(obj, dict):
        try:
            return json.dumps(obj, sort_keys=True, ensure_ascii=False)
        except Exception:
            return tuple(sorted((str(k), _hashable_key(v)) for k, v in obj.items()))
    if isinstance(obj, (list, tuple, set)):
        return tuple(_hashable_key(x) for x in obj)
    return obj if isinstance(obj, (str, int, float, bool, type(None))) else str(obj)

def _dedup_dicts(seq: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    seen: set = set()
    out: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
    for d in seq or []:
        k = _hashable_key(d)
        if k in seen:
            continue
        seen.add(k)
        out.append(d)
    return out

def explain_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Baut eine kurze Begründung/Erklärung mit optionalen Belegen.
    Wichtig: KEIN set(dict) – Dedup über hashbare Schlüssel.
    """
    msgs = state.get("messages") or []
    derived: Dict[str, Any] = state.get("derived") or {}
    citations: List[Dict[str, Any]] = state.get("citations") or []

    # Stabil deduplizieren (z. B. gleiche Quelle mehrfach)
    citations = _dedup_dicts(citations)

    reason = derived.get("reason") or derived.get("explain") or ""
    if not isinstance(reason, str):
        reason = str(reason or "")

    text = "Kurzbegründung:\n" + (reason.strip() or "Die Empfehlung basiert auf den erkannten Parametern und Regeln.")
    if citations:
        text += "\n\nQuellen/Belege:"
        for c in citations[:5]:
            src = c.get("source") or c.get("title") or c.get("url") or "Quelle"
            text += f"\n• {src}"

    return {
        **state,
        "messages": [AIMessage(content=text)],
        "phase": "explain",
        "citations": citations,
        "explanation": text,
    }

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/explain.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/explain.py =====
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
import json
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Tuple

from langchain_core.messages import AIMessage

log = logging.getLogger(__name__)

def _hashable_key(obj: Any) -> Any:
    if isinstance(obj, dict):
        try:
            return json.dumps(obj, sort_keys=True, ensure_ascii=False)
        except Exception:
            return tuple(sorted((str(k), _hashable_key(v)) for k, v in obj.items()))
    if isinstance(obj, (list, tuple, set)):
        return tuple(_hashable_key(x) for x in obj)
    return obj if isinstance(obj, (str, int, float, bool, type(None))) else str(obj)

def _dedup_dicts(seq: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    seen: set = set()
    out: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
    for d in seq or []:
        k = _hashable_key(d)
        if k in seen:
            continue
        seen.add(k)
        out.append(d)
    return out

def explain_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:

    if not isinstance(reason, str):

    if citations:

===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/intake.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/intake.py
from __future__ import annotations

import json
import logging
import re as _re
from typing import Any, Dict

from langchain_core.messages import HumanMessage, AIMessage
from app.services.langgraph.prompting import (
    render_template,
    messages_for_template,
    strip_json_fence,
)
from .. import utils
utils_mod = utils
# Vereinheitlichte LLM-Factory für Consult
from ..config import create_llm  # FIX: Nutzt fixierten create_llm

log = logging.getLogger("uvicorn.error")

def _safe_json_loads(_raw: str):
    """
    Erweitertes Parsing mit detailliertem Logging und Regex-Fallback.
    """
    if not _raw or not str(_raw).strip():
        log.warning("[intake] Empty raw response")
        return {}
    try:
        return json.loads(_raw)
    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
        log.warning("[intake] JSON decode error: %s on raw: %s", e, _raw[:200])
        m = _re.search(r'\{.*\}', str(_raw), _re.S)
        if m:
            try:
                parsed = json.loads(m.group(0))
                log.info("[intake] Regex fallback succeeded")
                return parsed
            except json.JSONDecodeError:
                log.error("[intake] Regex fallback failed")
                pass
        return {}  # Ultimate Fallback

def intake_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Analysiert die Eingabe, klassifiziert den Intent und extrahiert Parameter.
    Deterministischer Output: state['triage'], state['params'].
    Öffnet (falls Pflichtfelder fehlen) direkt die Sidebar-Form via ui_event.
    """
    try:
        msgs = utils_mod.normalize_messages(state.get("messages", []))
        params = dict(state.get("params") or {})

        prompt = render_template(
            "intake_triage.jinja2",
            messages=messages_for_template(msgs),
            params=params,
            params_json=json.dumps(params, ensure_ascii=False),
        )

        # Intake nutzt bewusst das leichtere GPT-5-Nano.
        llm = create_llm(streaming=False, model="gpt-4o-mini")  # FIX: Echtes LLM
        resp = llm.invoke([HumanMessage(content=prompt)])
        raw = strip_json_fence(getattr(resp, "content", "") or "")
        log.debug("[intake] Raw LLM response: %s", raw[:300])
        data = _safe_json_loads(raw)
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("intake_node: llm_or_parse_error: %s", e, exc_info=True)
        data = {}

    intent = str((data.get("intent") or "unknown")).strip().lower()
    # Dynamische Confidence basierend auf Data
    confidence = data.get("confidence", 1.0 if intent in ("greeting", "smalltalk", "consult") else 0.0)
    new_params = dict(params)
    if isinstance(data.get("params"), dict):
        for k, v in data["params"].items():
            if v not in (None, "", "unknown"):
                new_params[k] = v

    triage = {
        "intent": intent if intent in ("greeting", "smalltalk", "consult", "unknown") else "unknown",
        "confidence": float(confidence),
        "reply": "",
        "flags": {"source": "intake_triage"},
    }

    # Sidebar sofort öffnen, wenn Kern-Pflichtfelder fehlen
    domain_guess = "hydraulics_rod" if any(k in new_params for k in ("stange_mm", "nut_d_mm", "nut_b_mm")) else "rwdr"
    missing = utils_mod.missing_by_domain(domain_guess, new_params)

    ui_event = None
    assistant_msg = None
    if missing:
        example = (
            "Stange 25, Nut D 32, Nut B 6, Medium Öl, Tmax 80, Druck 160 bar, v 0,3 m/s"
            if domain_guess == "hydraulics_rod"
            else "Welle 25, Gehäuse 47, Breite 7, Medium Öl, Tmax 80, Druck 2 bar, n 1500"
        )
        optional_missing = utils_mod.optional_missing_by_domain(domain_guess, new_params)
        friendly_required = utils_mod.friendly_required_list(domain_guess, missing)
        friendly_optional = utils_mod.friendly_optional_list(domain_guess, optional_missing)
        friendly_legacy = friendly_required or ", ".join(missing)
        assistant_msg = AIMessage(
            content=render_template(
                "ask_missing.jinja2",
                domain=domain_guess,
                friendly=friendly_legacy,
                friendly_required=friendly_required,
                friendly_optional=friendly_optional,
                missing_required=missing,
                missing_optional=optional_missing,
                example=example,
                lang="de",
            )
        )
        ui_event = {
            "ui_action": "open_form",
            "form_id": f"{domain_guess}_params_v1",
            "schema_ref": f"domains/{domain_guess}/params@1.0.0",
            "missing": missing,
            "prefill": {k: v for k, v in new_params.items() if v not in (None, "", [])},
            "domain_guess": domain_guess,
        }
        log.info("[intake_node] early_open_form domain=%s missing=%s", domain_guess, missing)

    return {
        "messages": ([assistant_msg] if assistant_msg else []),
        "params": new_params,
        "triage": triage,
        "phase": "intake",
        **({"ui_event": ui_event} if ui_event else {}),
    }

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/intake.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/intake.py =====
