        "triage": triage,
        "phase": "intake",
        **({"ui_event": ui_event} if ui_event else {}),
    }

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/intake.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/intent_llm.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/intent_llm.py
from __future__ import annotations

import json
import logging
from typing import Any, Dict, List

from langchain_core.messages import HumanMessage, AIMessage, BaseMessage
from langchain_core.prompts import ChatPromptTemplate, MessagesPlaceholder

from app.services.langgraph.prompting import render_template
from app.services.langgraph.graph.consult.config import create_llm  # FIX: Nutzt fixierten LLM
from ...logging_utils import wrap_node_with_logging

log = logging.getLogger(__name__)

_GRAPH_NAME = "ConsultGraph"

# Prompt für Intent-Router (Jinja2-Template) – erweitert um Material-Detection
INTENT_PROMPT_TEMPLATE = """
Du bist ein Intent-Router für SealAI, eine KI-Plattform für Dichtungstechnik.

Analysiere die Nutzereingabe und klassifiziere den Intent:

- **smalltalk**: Reine Grüße, Smalltalk, Off-Topic, Tests wie "ping" oder "Hallo", "Wie geht's?".
- **consult**: Fachliche Queries zu Dichtungen, Materialien, Normen, Berechnungen (z.B. "Dichtung für Öl bei 80°C").
- Wenn Materialien wie PTFE, FKM, NBR erwähnt, setze "material_query": true und "intent": "consult".

Falls der Intent unklar ist, wähle "consult" als Default.

Gib als JSON zurück (streng!):
{{
  "intent": "smalltalk" oder "consult",
  "confidence": 0.0-1.0,
  "reason": "Kurze Begründung",
  "material_query": true/false
}}

Nutzereingabe: {{ input_text }}
Vorherige Nachrichten: {{ messages | tojson }}
"""

def _extract_input_text(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    """
    Extrahiert den Input-Text aus State.
    FIX: Handhabt sowohl dict als auch LangChain Messages (z.B. HumanMessage).
    Priorisiert den neuesten User-Input.
    """
    # 1) Direkter Input
    inp = state.get("input") or state.get("question") or state.get("user_input")
    if isinstance(inp, str) and inp.strip():
        return inp.strip()

    # 2) Letzte User-/Human-Message (handhabt dict und Message-Objekte)
    msgs = state.get("messages", [])
    if isinstance(msgs, list) and msgs:
        for m in reversed(msgs):
            if isinstance(m, dict):
                role = (m.get("role") or m.get("type") or "").lower()
                content = m.get("content", "")
            else:  # FIX: LangChain Message (z.B. HumanMessage)
                try:
                    role = getattr(m, "role", getattr(m, "type", "")).lower()
                    content = getattr(m, "content", "")
                except AttributeError:
                    continue

            if role in {"user", "human"} and isinstance(content, str) and content.strip():
                return content.strip()

    # 3) Fallback: Join aller Contents
    parts = []
    for m in msgs:
        if isinstance(m, dict):
            c = m.get("content", "")
        else:
            try:
                c = getattr(m, "content", "")
            except AttributeError:
                continue
        if isinstance(c, str) and c.strip():
            parts.append(c.strip())
    return " ".join(parts) if parts else ""

def _normalize_text(text: str) -> str:
    return text.strip().lower() if text else ""

def intent_router_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    LLM-basierter Intent-Router: Klassifiziert nach Smalltalk vs. Consult.
    FIX: Erweitert um material_query Flag für besseres Recognition.
    """
    try:
        input_text = _extract_input_text(state)
        if not input_text:
            log.warning("[intent_router] No input text found in state")
            return {**state, "route": "consult", "phase": "intent_router"}  # Default zu Consult

        # Render Prompt
        prompt = render_template(
            "intent_router.jinja2",  # Annahme: Template existiert; passe an INTENT_PROMPT_TEMPLATE an
            input_text=input_text,
            messages=state.get("messages", []),
        )

        # LLM-Aufruf (FIX: Echtes Runnable)
        llm = create_llm(streaming=False, model="gpt-4o-mini")
        messages = [HumanMessage(content=prompt)]
        resp = llm.invoke(messages)
        content = getattr(resp, "content", "").strip()

        log.info("[intent_router] Prompt sent to LLM: %s", prompt[:100] + "..." if len(prompt) > 100 else prompt)  # FIX: Logging für Übertragung

        # Parse JSON-Response
        try:
            data = json.loads(content)
            intent = str(data.get("intent", "consult")).strip().lower()
            confidence = float(data.get("confidence", 0.5))
            reason = str(data.get("reason", ""))
            material_query = bool(data.get("material_query", False))
        except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError) as e:
            log.warning("[intent_router] Parse error: %s on %s", e, content[:100])
            intent = "consult"  # Default
            confidence = 0.5
            reason = "Parse failed"
            material_query = False

        # FIX: Mappe ungültige Intents wie "routing_error" zu "consult"
        if intent not in ["smalltalk", "consult"]:
            intent = "consult"
            reason += " (mapped from invalid intent)"

        log.info("[intent_router] Intent=%s (conf=%.2f, material_query=%s): %s", intent, confidence, material_query, reason)

        new_state = dict(state)
        new_state["route"] = "smalltalk" if intent == "smalltalk" else "consult"
        new_state["intent_confidence"] = confidence
        new_state["intent_reason"] = reason
        new_state["material_query"] = material_query  # FIX: Flag für nachfolgende Nodes
        new_state["phase"] = "intent_router"

        # Assistant-Message hinzufügen (optional, für Trace)
        assistant_msg = AIMessage(content=f"Intent: {intent} (conf: {confidence:.2f})")
        new_state["messages"] = new_state.get("messages", []) + [assistant_msg]

        return new_state
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[intent_router] Error: %s", e)
        return {**state, "route": "consult", "phase": "intent_router"}  # Recovery: Default zu Consult

# Wrapper für Logging
intent_router_node = wrap_node_with_logging(_GRAPH_NAME, "intent_router", intent_router_node)

__all__ = ["intent_router_node"]

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/intent_llm.py =====

from langchain_core.prompts import ChatPromptTemplate, MessagesPlaceholder

from app.services.langgraph.graph.consult.config import create_llm  # FIX: Nutzt fixierten LLM

===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/lite_router.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/lite_router.py
from __future__ import annotations
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional
import re
import unicodedata
import structlog
import logging  # Für erweitertes Logging

log = structlog.get_logger(__name__)

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# Heuristiken / Schlüsselwörter
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

GREETINGS = {
    "hi", "hallo", "hey", "moin", "servus", "guten tag", "guten morgen",
    "guten abend", "grüß dich", "gruss dich", "huhu"
}

# Fachsignale (Werkstoffe, Dichtung, Maße, Betriebsbedingungen, Normen)
DOMAIN_KEYWORDS = {
    # Werkstoffe
    "ptfe", "fkm", "viton", "nbr", "epdm", "hnbr", "ffkm", "peek", "pvdf",
    # Komponenten / Produkte
    "dichtung", "o-ring", "oring", "stangendichtung", "kolbendichtung",
    "nut", "nutmaß", "nutmass", "nutbreite", "durchmesser", "profil",
    # Betriebsbedingungen / Normen
    "druck", "bar", "temperatur", "°c", "grad", "medium", "medien",
    "chemie", "chemikalie", "säure", "öl", "fda", "iso", "din", "en",
    # Entscheidungs-/Vergleichs-Signale
    "vergleiche", "vergleich", "gegenüberstellung", "empfehlung",
    "auswahl", "werkstoffauswahl", "materialauswahl",
}

UNIT_PATTERNS = [
    r"\b\d+(\,\d+)?\s*mm\b",
    r"\b\d+(\,\d+)?\s*bar\b",
    r"\b\d+(\,\d+)?\s*°c\b",
]

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# Utilities
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

def _normalize(text: str) -> str:
    t = unicodedata.normalize("NFKC", text or "")
    return t.lower().strip()

def _last_user_text(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    """
    Nimmt den sinnvollsten Text für die Routing-Entscheidung:
    - state['input'] bevorzugt
    - sonst letzte user/human message
    - fallback: join aller message contents
    """
    # FIX: Besserer Fallback für leere States
    if not state:
        log.warning("[lite_router] Empty state")
        return ""
    
    # 1) Direkter Input
    inp = state.get("input") or state.get("question") or state.get("user_input")
    if isinstance(inp, str) and inp.strip():
        return inp.strip()

    # 2) Letzte User-/Human-Message
    msgs = state.get("messages")
    if isinstance(msgs, list) and msgs:
        for m in reversed(msgs):
            if isinstance(m, dict):
                role = _normalize(str(m.get("role") or m.get("type") or ""))
                content = m.get("content")
                if role in {"user", "human"} and isinstance(content, str) and content.strip():
                    return content.strip()
            else:
                try:
                    content = getattr(m, "content", None)
                    if isinstance(content, str) and content.strip():
                        return content.strip()
                except Exception:
                    pass

    # 3) Fallback
    if isinstance(msgs, list):
        parts: List[str] = []
        for m in msgs:
            if isinstance(m, dict):
                c = m.get("content")
                if isinstance(c, str) and c.strip():
                    parts.append(c.strip())
        if parts:
            return " ".join(parts)
    return ""

def _looks_like_greeting(t: str) -> bool:
    if not t:
        return False
    n = _normalize(t)
    if n in GREETINGS:
        return True
    # sehr kurze Opener
    return len(n) <= 6 and any(g in n for g in GREETINGS)

def _has_domain_signals(t: str) -> bool:
    if not t:
        return False
    n = _normalize(t)

    # harte Schlüsselwörter
    for kw in DOMAIN_KEYWORDS:
        if kw in n:
            return True

    # Maße/Einheiten
    for pat in UNIT_PATTERNS:
        if re.search(pat, n):
            return True

    # simple chemische Formeln
    if re.search(r"\b(h2so4|hno3|hcl|naoh|h3po4|ch3|c2h5|c3h7)\b", n):
        return True

    # Vergleichsanfragen
    if " vs " in n or " gegen " in n or " versus " in n:
        return True

    return False

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# Router-Logik
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

def route(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Entscheidet, ob in 'smalltalk' oder in den Intake-/Consult-Pfad
    geroutet wird. Der Build liest 'route' vom State und hat eine Kante
    'lite_router.route -> <edge-name>'.
    """
    text = _last_user_text(state)
    ntext = _normalize(text)

    # 1) Fachsignale -> Intake (weiterer Flow: Intake/Ask-Missing -> RAG -> Recommend)
    if _has_domain_signals(ntext):
        dest = "default"  # FIX: Mappe zu 'default' für conditional_edges
        log.info("[lite_router] route=INTAKE", text=text[:50] + "..." if len(text) > 50 else text)
        out = dict(state)
        out.update({"route": dest, "phase": "lite_router"})
        return out

    # 2) reine kurze Grüße -> Smalltalk
    if _looks_like_greeting(ntext):
        dest = "smalltalk"
        log.info("[lite_router] route=SMALLTALK", text=text[:50] + "..." if len(text) > 50 else text)
        out = dict(state)
        out.update({"route": dest, "phase": "lite_router"})
        return out

    # 3) Default: lieber Intake als Smalltalk
    dest = "default"  # FIX: Mappe zu 'default' für conditional_edges
    log.info("[lite_router] route=INTAKE(default)", text=text[:50] + "..." if len(text) > 50 else text)
    out = dict(state)
    out.update({"route": dest, "phase": "lite_router"})
    return out

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# Node-Factory, die vom Build importiert wird
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

def lite_router_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Wrapper, damit build.py weiterhin `lite_router_node` importieren kann.
    Entspricht einem einfachen Funktions-Node in eurer State-Maschine.
    """
    return route(state)


__all__ = ["lite_router_node", "route"]

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/lite_router.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/lite_router.py =====

    'lite_router.route -> <edge-name>'.

        out.update({"route": dest, "phase": "lite_router"})
        return out

    # 3) Default: lieber Intake als Smalltalk
    dest = "default"  # FIX: Mappe zu 'default' für conditional_edges
    log.info("[lite_router] route=INTAKE(default)", text=text[:50] + "..." if len(text) > 50 else text)
    out = dict(state)
    out.update({"route": dest, "phase": "lite_router"})
    return out

# -------------------------------------------------------------------
# Node-Factory, die vom Build importiert wird
# -------------------------------------------------------------------

def lite_router_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Wrapper, damit build.py weiterhin `lite_router_node` importieren kann.
    Entspricht einem einfachen Funktions-Node in eurer State-Maschine.
    """
    return route(state)


__all__ = ["lite_router_node", "route"]

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/lite_router.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/ltm.py =====
from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

from ....tools import long_term_memory as ltm


def _extract_query(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    q = (state.get("query") or state.get("question") or state.get("input") or "").strip()
    if q:
        return q
    # fallback: last human text from messages
    msgs = state.get("messages") or []
    for m in reversed(msgs):
        role = (getattr(m, "type", "") or getattr(m, "role", "") or "").lower()
        content = getattr(m, "content", "")
        if isinstance(m, dict):
            role = (m.get("type") or m.get("role") or "").lower()
            content = m.get("content")
        if role in ("human", "user") and isinstance(content, str) and content.strip():
            return content.strip()
    return ""


def ltm_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """Augment state.context with user-specific LTM context from Qdrant.

    Inputs:
      - query (preferred) or last user message
      - user_id, chat_id (optional for filtering)
    Outputs:
      - context: concatenated LTM context + existing context
      - ltm_hits: optional raw hits for debugging/inspection
    """
    query = _extract_query(state)
    if not query:
        return {**state, "phase": "ltm"}

    user_id = state.get("user_id") or None
    chat_id = state.get("chat_id") or None

    ctx, hits = ltm.ltm_query(query, user=user_id, chat_id=chat_id, top_k=5, strategy="mmr")

    existing_ctx = state.get("context") or ""
    if isinstance(existing_ctx, dict):
        existing_ctx = ""
    if not isinstance(existing_ctx, str):
        existing_ctx = ""

    new_ctx_parts: List[str] = []
    if ctx:
        new_ctx_parts.append(ctx)
    if existing_ctx:
        new_ctx_parts.append(existing_ctx)
    merged_ctx = "\n\n".join([p for p in new_ctx_parts if p])

    out = {**state, "phase": "ltm"}
    if merged_ctx:
        out["context"] = merged_ctx
    # keep raw hits for optional downstream use
    out["ltm_hits"] = hits
    return out


__all__ = ["ltm_node"]


===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/ltm.py =====

===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/profile.py =====
from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Any, Dict, List

from ....tools.profile_loader import get_user_profile, profile_to_context


def profile_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """Load user profile from Postgres (if available) and inject into state.

    - Sets state.user_profile
    - Merges profile params_patch into state.params (shallow)
    - Appends a compact profile context to state.context
    """
    user_id = state.get("user_id") or None
    profile = get_user_profile(user_id)
    if not profile:
        return {**state, "phase": "profile"}

    out: Dict[str, Any] = {**state, "user_profile": profile, "phase": "profile"}

    # Merge params_patch into params
    if isinstance(profile.get("params_patch"), dict):
        params = dict(out.get("params") or {})
        for k, v in profile["params_patch"].items():
            params.setdefault(k, v)
        out["params"] = params

    # Context augmentation
    ctx = profile_to_context(profile)
    if ctx:
        existing = out.get("context") or ""
        if not isinstance(existing, str):
            existing = ""
        merged = "\n\n".join([p for p in [ctx, existing] if p])
        out["context"] = merged

    return out


__all__ = ["profile_node"]


===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/profile.py =====

# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/rag.py
"""
RAG-Node: holt Hybrid-Treffer (Qdrant + Redis BM25), baut kompakten
Kontext-String und legt beides in den State (retrieved_docs/docs, context) ab.
"""
from __future__ import annotations
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional
import structlog

# FIX: absoluter Import statt relativer
from app.services.rag import rag_orchestrator as ro

log = structlog.get_logger(__name__)

def _extract_query(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    return (
        state.get("query")
        or state.get("question")
        or state.get("user_input")
        or state.get("input")
        or ""
    )

def _extract_tenant(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Optional[str]:
    ctx = state.get("context") or {}
    return state.get("tenant") or (ctx.get("tenant") if isinstance(ctx, dict) else None)

def _context_from_docs(docs: List[Dict[str, Any]], max_chars: int = 1200) -> str:
    """Kompakter Textkontext für Prompting (inkl. Quelle)."""
    if not docs:
        return ""
    parts: List[str] = []
    for d in docs[:6]:
        t = (d.get("text") or "").strip()
        if not t:
            continue
        src = d.get("source") or (d.get("metadata") or {}).get("source")
        if src:
            t = f"{t}\n[source: {src}]"
        parts.append(t)
    ctx = "\n\n".join(parts)
    return ctx[:max_chars]

def run_rag_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Eingänge (optional):
      - query/question/user_input/input
      - tenant bzw. context.tenant
      - rag_filters, rag_k, rag_rerank
    Ausgänge:
      - retrieved_docs/docs: List[Dict[str, Any]]
      - context: str
    """

    query = _extract_query(state)
    # Hybrid Retrieval: Dense + Graph
    use_graph = True  # Config for GraphRAG
    if use_graph:
        # Placeholder for GraphRAG: Simulate graph-based search
        graph_docs = _graph_rag_search(query, state)
        dense_docs = _dense_rag_search(query, state)
        retrieved_docs = graph_docs + dense_docs  # Combine
    else:
        retrieved_docs = _dense_rag_search(query, state)

    tenant = _extract_tenant(state)
    filters = state.get("rag_filters") or None
    k = int(state.get("rag_k") or ro.FINAL_K)
    use_rerank = bool(state.get("rag_rerank", True))

    if not query.strip():
        return {**state, "retrieved_docs": [], "docs": [], "context": "", "phase": "rag"}

    docs = ro.hybrid_retrieve(
        query=query,
        tenant=tenant,
        k=k,
        metadata_filters=filters,
        use_rerank=use_rerank,
    )

    context = state.get("context")
    if not isinstance(context, str) or not context.strip():
        context = _context_from_docs(docs)

    out = {
        **state,
        "retrieved_docs": docs,
        "docs": docs,  # Alias für nachfolgende Nodes
        "context": context,
        "phase": "rag",
    }
    try:
        log.info("[rag_node] retrieved", n=len(docs), tenant=tenant or "-", ctx_len=len(context or ""))
    except Exception:
        pass
    return out

__all__ = ["run_rag_node"]

def _graph_rag_search(query: str, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """Placeholder for GraphRAG search."""
    # Simulate graph traversal for related concepts
    # In real impl, use Neo4j or similar
    return [{"text": f"GraphRAG result for {query}: Related concept A", "source": "graph"}]

def _dense_rag_search(query: str, state: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """Existing dense search logic."""
    # Placeholder, integrate existing logic
    return [{"text": f"Dense result for {query}", "source": "dense"}]

# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/recommend.py
from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
import re
from typing import Any, Callable, Dict, List, Optional

import structlog
from langchain_core.messages import AIMessage, SystemMessage
from langchain_core.runnables.config import RunnableConfig

from app.services.langgraph.prompting import (
    render_template,
    messages_for_template,
    strip_json_fence,
)
from app.services.langgraph.prompt_registry import get_agent_prompt
from app.services.langgraph.prompting import build_system_prompt_from_parts
from .. import utils as utils_mod
from ..config import create_llm
from ..utils.parsing import parse_recommendations

log = structlog.get_logger(__name__)

_STREAM_CHUNK_CHARS = 160

def _extract_text_from_chunk(chunk) -> List[str]:
    out: List[str] = []
    if not chunk:
        return out
    c = getattr(chunk, "content", None)
    if isinstance(c, str) and c:
        out.append(c)
    elif isinstance(c, list):
        for part in c:
            if isinstance(part, str):
                out.append(part)
            elif isinstance(part, dict) and isinstance(part.get("text"), str):
                out.append(part["text"])
    ak = getattr(chunk, "additional_kwargs", None)
    if isinstance(ak, dict):
        for k in ("delta", "content", "text", "token"):
            v = ak.get(k)
            if isinstance(v, str) and v:
                out.append(v)
    if isinstance(chunk, dict):
        for k in ("delta", "content", "text", "token"):
            v = chunk.get(k)
            if isinstance(v, str) and v:
                out.append(v)
    return out
def recommend_node(
    state: Dict[str, Any],
    config: Optional[RunnableConfig] = None,
    *,
    events: Optional[Callable[[Dict[str, Any]], None]] = None,
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    # Falls noch Pflichtfelder fehlen, NICHT ins teure RAG/LLM gehen – stattdessen UI-Form öffnen
    msgs = utils_mod.normalize_messages(state.get("messages", []))
    missing = state.get("fehlend") or state.get("missing") or []
    if isinstance(missing, (list, tuple)) and len(missing) > 0:
        missing_list = ", ".join(str(item) for item in missing)
        hint = (
            "Mir fehlen noch Angaben (" + missing_list + ") – bitte die Formularfelder ergänzen." if missing_list else
            "Mir fehlen noch konkrete Angaben – bitte die Formularfelder ergänzen."
        )
        ui = {
            "ui_event": {
                "ui_action": "open_form",
                "form_id": "rwdr_params_v1",
                "schema_ref": "domains/rwdr/params@1.0.0",
                "missing": list(missing),
                "prefill": (state.get("params") or {})
            }
        }
        ai_msg = AIMessage(content=hint)
        return {
            **state,
            **ui,
            "phase": "ask_missing",
            "messages": msgs + [ai_msg],
            "missing_fields": list(missing),
        }
    params: Dict[str, Any] = state.get("params") or {}
    domain = (state.get("domain") or "").strip().lower()
    derived = state.get("derived") or {}
    retrieved_docs: List[Dict[str, Any]] = state.get("retrieved_docs") or []
    context = state.get("context") or _context_from_docs(retrieved_docs)
    if context:
        log.info("[recommend_node] using_context", n_docs=len(retrieved_docs), ctx_len=len(context))

    try:
        base_llm = create_llm(streaming=True)
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[recommend_node] llm_factory_failed", err=str(e))
        fallback_payload = json.dumps({"empfehlungen": []}, ensure_ascii=False, separators=(",", ":"))
        ai_msg = AIMessage(
            content="Es tut mir leid – der Empfehlungsdienst ist momentan nicht verfügbar. Bitte versuchen Sie es später erneut."
        )
        return {
            **state,
            "messages": msgs + [ai_msg],
            "answer": fallback_payload,
            "phase": "recommend",
            "empfehlungen": [],
            "retrieved_docs": state.get("retrieved_docs") or [],
            "docs": state.get("retrieved_docs") or [],
            "context": state.get("context") or "",
        }

    try:
        llm = base_llm.bind(response_format={"type": "json_object"})
    except Exception:
        llm = base_llm

    recent_user = (utils_mod.last_user_text(msgs) or "").strip()
    prompt = render_template(
        "recommend.jinja2",
        messages=messages_for_template(msgs),
        params=params,
        domain=domain,
        derived=derived,
        recent_user=recent_user,
        context=context,
    )

    effective_cfg: RunnableConfig = (config or {}).copy()  # type: ignore[assignment]
    if "run_name" not in (effective_cfg or {}):
        effective_cfg = {**effective_cfg, "run_name": "recommend"}  # type: ignore[dict-item]

    content_parts: List[str] = []
    # Combine domain/system prompt and the generated prompt into a single system message
    domain_prompt = get_agent_prompt(domain or "rwdr")
    # retrieved_docs may contain dicts with "text"
    rag_texts = [d.get("text") for d in retrieved_docs if isinstance(d, dict) and d.get("text")]
    system_text = build_system_prompt_from_parts(
        f"{domain_prompt}\n\n{prompt}",
        summary=None,
        rag_docs=rag_texts,
        max_tokens=int(os.getenv("PROMPT_MAX_TOKENS", "3000")),
        model=os.getenv("OPENAI_MODEL", "gpt-4o"),
    )
    try:
        for chunk in llm.with_config(effective_cfg).stream([
            SystemMessage(content=system_text),
        ]):
            texts = _extract_text_from_chunk(chunk)
            for piece in texts:
                _emit_stream_chunks(events, node="recommend", text=piece)
            content_parts.extend(texts)
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning("[recommend_node] stream_failed", err=str(e))
        try:
            resp = llm.invoke([
                SystemMessage(content=system_text),
            ], config=effective_cfg)
            final_text = getattr(resp, "content", "") or ""
            if final_text:
                _emit_stream_chunks(events, node="recommend", text=final_text)
            content_parts = [final_text]
        except Exception as e2:
            log.error("[recommend_node] invoke_failed", err=str(e2))
            payload = json.dumps({"empfehlungen": []}, ensure_ascii=False, separators=(",", ":"))
            _emit_stream_chunks(events, node="recommend", text=payload)
            ai_msg = AIMessage(content=payload)
            return {
                **state,
                "messages": msgs + [ai_msg],
                "answer": payload,
                "phase": "recommend",
                "empfehlungen": [],
                "retrieved_docs": retrieved_docs,
                "docs": retrieved_docs,
                "context": context,
            }

    raw = ("".join(content_parts) or "").strip()
    log.info("[recommend_node] stream_len", chars=len(raw))

    recs = parse_recommendations(raw)

    content_out = json.dumps({"empfehlungen": recs}, ensure_ascii=False, separators=(",", ":")).replace("\n", " ").strip()

    ai_msg = AIMessage(content=content_out)
    return {
        **state,
        "messages": msgs + [ai_msg],
        "answer": content_out,
        "phase": "recommend",
        "empfehlungen": recs,
        "retrieved_docs": retrieved_docs,
        "docs": retrieved_docs,
        "context": context,
    }

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/recommend.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/recommend.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/recommend.py
from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
import re
from typing import Any, Callable, Dict, List, Optional

import structlog
from langchain_core.messages import AIMessage, SystemMessage
from langchain_core.runnables.config import RunnableConfig

from app.services.langgraph.prompting import (
    render_template,
    messages_for_template,
    strip_json_fence,
)
from app.services.langgraph.prompt_registry import get_agent_prompt
from app.services.langgraph.prompting import build_system_prompt_from_parts
from .. import utils as utils_mod
from ..config import create_llm
from ..utils.parsing import parse_recommendations

log = structlog.get_logger(__name__)

_STREAM_CHUNK_CHARS = 160

def _extract_text_from_chunk(chunk) -> List[str]:
    out: List[str] = []
    if not chunk:
        return out
    c = getattr(chunk, "content", None)
    if isinstance(c, str) and c:
        out.append(c)
    elif isinstance(c, list):
        for part in c:
            if isinstance(part, str):
                out.append(part)
            elif isinstance(part, dict) and isinstance(part.get("text"), str):
                out.append(part["text"])
    ak = getattr(chunk, "additional_kwargs", None)
    if isinstance(ak, dict):
        for k in ("delta", "content", "text", "token"):
            v = ak.get(k)
            if isinstance(v, str) and v:
                out.append(v)
    if isinstance(chunk, dict):
        for k in ("delta", "content", "text", "token"):
            v = chunk.get(k)
            if isinstance(v, str) and v:
                out.append(v)
    return out
def recommend_node(
    state: Dict[str, Any],
    config: Optional[RunnableConfig] = None,
    *,
    events: Optional[Callable[[Dict[str, Any]], None]] = None,
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    # Falls noch Pflichtfelder fehlen, NICHT ins teure RAG/LLM gehen – stattdessen UI-Form öffnen
    msgs = utils_mod.normalize_messages(state.get("messages", []))
    missing = state.get("fehlend") or state.get("missing") or []
    if isinstance(missing, (list, tuple)) and len(missing) > 0:
        missing_list = ", ".join(str(item) for item in missing)
        hint = (
            "Mir fehlen noch Angaben (" + missing_list + ") – bitte die Formularfelder ergänzen." if missing_list else
            "Mir fehlen noch konkrete Angaben – bitte die Formularfelder ergänzen."
        )
        ui = {
            "ui_event": {
                "ui_action": "open_form",
                "form_id": "rwdr_params_v1",
                "schema_ref": "domains/rwdr/params@1.0.0",
                "missing": list(missing),
                "prefill": (state.get("params") or {})
            }
        }
        ai_msg = AIMessage(content=hint)
        return {
            **state,
            **ui,
            "phase": "ask_missing",
            "messages": msgs + [ai_msg],
            "missing_fields": list(missing),
        }
    params: Dict[str, Any] = state.get("params") or {}
    domain = (state.get("domain") or "").strip().lower()
    derived = state.get("derived") or {}
    retrieved_docs: List[Dict[str, Any]] = state.get("retrieved_docs") or []
    context = state.get("context") or _context_from_docs(retrieved_docs)
    if context:
        log.info("[recommend_node] using_context", n_docs=len(retrieved_docs), ctx_len=len(context))

    try:
        base_llm = create_llm(streaming=True)
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[recommend_node] llm_factory_failed", err=str(e))
        fallback_payload = json.dumps({"empfehlungen": []}, ensure_ascii=False, separators=(",", ":"))
        ai_msg = AIMessage(
            content="Es tut mir leid – der Empfehlungsdienst ist momentan nicht verfügbar. Bitte versuchen Sie es später erneut."
        )
        return {
            **state,
            "messages": msgs + [ai_msg],
            "answer": fallback_payload,
            "phase": "recommend",
            "empfehlungen": [],
            "retrieved_docs": state.get("retrieved_docs") or [],
            "docs": state.get("retrieved_docs") or [],
            "context": state.get("context") or "",
        }

    try:
        llm = base_llm.bind(response_format={"type": "json_object"})
    except Exception:
        llm = base_llm

    recent_user = (utils_mod.last_user_text(msgs) or "").strip()
    prompt = render_template(
        "recommend.jinja2",
        messages=messages_for_template(msgs),
        params=params,
        domain=domain,
        derived=derived,
        recent_user=recent_user,
        context=context,
    )

    effective_cfg: RunnableConfig = (config or {}).copy()  # type: ignore[assignment]
    if "run_name" not in (effective_cfg or {}):
        effective_cfg = {**effective_cfg, "run_name": "recommend"}  # type: ignore[dict-item]

    content_parts: List[str] = []
    # Combine domain/system prompt and the generated prompt into a single system message
    domain_prompt = get_agent_prompt(domain or "rwdr")
    # retrieved_docs may contain dicts with "text"
    rag_texts = [d.get("text") for d in retrieved_docs if isinstance(d, dict) and d.get("text")]
    system_text = build_system_prompt_from_parts(
        f"{domain_prompt}\n\n{prompt}",
        summary=None,
        rag_docs=rag_texts,
        max_tokens=int(os.getenv("PROMPT_MAX_TOKENS", "3000")),
        model=os.getenv("OPENAI_MODEL", "gpt-4o"),
    )
    try:
        for chunk in llm.with_config(effective_cfg).stream([
            SystemMessage(content=system_text),
        ]):
            texts = _extract_text_from_chunk(chunk)
            for piece in texts:
                _emit_stream_chunks(events, node="recommend", text=piece)
            content_parts.extend(texts)
    except Exception as e:
        log.warning("[recommend_node] stream_failed", err=str(e))
        try:
            resp = llm.invoke([
                SystemMessage(content=system_text),
            ], config=effective_cfg)
            final_text = getattr(resp, "content", "") or ""
            if final_text:
                _emit_stream_chunks(events, node="recommend", text=final_text)
            content_parts = [final_text]
        except Exception as e2:
            log.error("[recommend_node] invoke_failed", err=str(e2))
            payload = json.dumps({"empfehlungen": []}, ensure_ascii=False, separators=(",", ":"))
            _emit_stream_chunks(events, node="recommend", text=payload)
            ai_msg = AIMessage(content=payload)
            return {
                **state,
                "messages": msgs + [ai_msg],
                "answer": payload,
                "phase": "recommend",
                "empfehlungen": [],
                "retrieved_docs": retrieved_docs,
                "docs": retrieved_docs,
                "context": context,
            }

    raw = ("".join(content_parts) or "").strip()
    log.info("[recommend_node] stream_len", chars=len(raw))

    recs = parse_recommendations(raw)

    content_out = json.dumps({"empfehlungen": recs}, ensure_ascii=False, separators=(",", ":")).replace("\n", " ").strip()

    ai_msg = AIMessage(content=content_out)
    return {
        **state,
        "messages": msgs + [ai_msg],
        "answer": content_out,
        "phase": "recommend",
        "empfehlungen": recs,
        "retrieved_docs": retrieved_docs,
        "docs": retrieved_docs,
        "context": context,
    }

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/recommend.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/smalltalk.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/smalltalk.py
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from typing import Any, Dict, List

from langchain_core.messages import HumanMessage, AIMessage
from app.services.langgraph.prompting import render_template
from app.services.langgraph.graph.consult.config import create_llm  # LLM-Factory
from ...logging_utils import wrap_node_with_logging  # Wrapper für Logging

log = logging.getLogger("uvicorn.error")

_GRAPH_NAME = "ConsultGraph"

# ============================================================
# Prompt-Template für Smalltalk (Jinja2)
# ============================================================
SMALLTALK_PROMPT_TEMPLATE = """
Du bist SealAI, eine freundliche KI-Spezialistin für Dichtungstechnik. Du führst ein lockeres Gespräch, aber lenkst es sanft zum Thema Dichtungen.

Regeln:
- Antworte natürlich und empathisch auf {{ input_text }}.
- Halte es kurz und positiv (1-2 Sätze).
- Füge immer eine offene Nachfrage zum Grund des Besuchs hinzu, z.B. "Wie kann ich bei Dichtungen oder Materialien helfen?" oder "Hast du eine Frage zu Normen oder Auswahl?".
- Bleibe im Kontext der Branche, aber sei nicht aufdringlich.

Vorherige Nachrichten: {{ messages | tojson }}

Antwort als AIMessage-Content (kein JSON).
"""

def _extract_input_text(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    """
    Extrahiert den Input-Text aus State (ähnlich wie in intent_llm.py).
    """
    # 1) Direkter Input
    inp = state.get("input") or state.get("question") or state.get("user_input")
    if isinstance(inp, str) and inp.strip():
        return inp.strip()

    # 2) Letzte User-/Human-Message
    msgs = state.get("messages", [])
    if isinstance(msgs, list) and msgs:
        for m in reversed(msgs):
            if isinstance(m, dict):
                role = (m.get("role") or m.get("type") or "").lower()
                content = m.get("content", "")
            else:
                try:
                    role = getattr(m, "role", getattr(m, "type", "")).lower()
                    content = getattr(m, "content", "")
                except AttributeError:
                    continue

            if role in {"user", "human"} and isinstance(content, str) and content.strip():
                return content.strip()

    # 3) Fallback
    parts = []
    for m in msgs:
        if isinstance(m, dict):
            c = m.get("content", "")
        else:
            try:
                c = getattr(m, "content", "")
            except AttributeError:
                continue
        if isinstance(c, str) and c.strip():
            parts.append(c.strip())
    return " ".join(parts) if parts else "Hallo! Ich bin SealAI."

def smalltalk_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Smalltalk-Node: LLM-generierte Antwort auf Input + offene Nachfrage zum Grund des Besuchs.
    FIX: Erweitert mit LLM für natürliche, kontextuelle Response.
    """
    try:
        input_text = _extract_input_text(state)
        if not input_text:
            log.warning("[smalltalk_node] No input text found in state")
            fallback_msg = AIMessage(content="Hallo! Ich bin SealAI, deine KI für Dichtungstechnik. Wie kann ich bei Materialien oder Normen helfen?")
            return {**state, "messages": state.get("messages", []) + [fallback_msg], "phase": "smalltalk_done"}

        # Render Prompt
        prompt = render_template(
            "smalltalk.jinja2",  # Jinja2-Template für smalltalk
            input_text=input_text,
            messages=state.get("messages", []),
        )

        # LLM-Aufruf
        llm = create_llm(streaming=False, model="gpt-4o-mini")  # Leichtes Modell für Smalltalk
        resp = llm.invoke([HumanMessage(content=prompt)])
        content = getattr(resp, "content", "").strip() or "Hallo! Ich bin SealAI. Wie kann ich bei Dichtungen helfen?"

        log.info("[smalltalk_node] Prompt: %s | Response: %s", prompt[:100], content[:100])

        # Assistant-Message hinzufügen
        assistant_msg = AIMessage(content=content)
        new_state = dict(state)
        new_state["messages"] = new_state.get("messages", []) + [assistant_msg]
        new_state["phase"] = "smalltalk_done"

        return new_state
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[smalltalk_node] Error: %s", e)
        fallback_msg = AIMessage(content="Hallo! Mir geht's gut – und dir? Wie kann ich bei Dichtungstechnik unterstützen?")
        return {**state, "messages": state.get("messages", []) + [fallback_msg], "phase": "smalltalk_done"}

# Wrapper für Logging
smalltalk_node = wrap_node_with_logging(_GRAPH_NAME, "smalltalk", smalltalk_node)

__all__ = ["smalltalk_node"]

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/smalltalk.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/smalltalk.py =====

===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/summarize.py =====
from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Any, Dict, List

from langchain_core.messages import AIMessage, HumanMessage

from ....llm_factory import get_llm
from ..memory_utils import set_summary
from ....tools import long_term_memory as ltm


def _last_user_text(messages: List[Any]) -> str:
    for m in reversed(messages or []):
        role = (getattr(m, "type", "") or getattr(m, "role", "") or "").lower()
        content = getattr(m, "content", "")
        if isinstance(m, dict):
            role = (m.get("type") or m.get("role") or "").lower()
            content = m.get("content")
        if role in ("human", "user") and isinstance(content, str) and content.strip():
            return content.strip()
    return ""


def summarize_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Erzeugt eine knappe Zusammenfassung (Context handoff), injiziert sie in STM
    und persistiert sie im LTM (Qdrant) als conversation_summary.

    Inputs:
      - messages, retrieved_docs/docs, user_id, chat_id
    Outputs:
      - summary_text (optional)
    Nebenwirkungen:
      - Redis: chat:stm:{thread}:summary
      - Qdrant LTM: kind=conversation_summary
    """
    try:
        llm = get_llm(streaming=False)
    except Exception:
        llm = None

    msgs = state.get("messages") or []
    docs = state.get("retrieved_docs") or state.get("docs") or []
    user_id = state.get("user_id") or state.get("tenant") or None
    chat_id = state.get("chat_id") or None

    # Baue knappen Prompt
    question = _last_user_text(msgs)
    context_parts: List[str] = []
    if isinstance(docs, list) and docs:
        for d in docs[:4]:
            t = (d.get("text") or "").strip()
            if t:
                context_parts.append(t)
    ctx_text = "\n\n".join(context_parts)[:800]

    summary_text = ""
    if llm is not None:
        prompt = (
            "Fasse den Gesprächsverlauf und die wichtigsten Fakten extrem kurz zusammen. "
            "Max 3 Sätze, Deutsch. Wenn vorhanden, Parameter (z.B. Temperatur, Druck) erwähnen.\n\n"
        )
        try:
            content = prompt
            if question:
                content += f"Letzte Frage: {question}\n"
            if ctx_text:
                content += f"Kontext: {ctx_text}\n"
            resp = llm.invoke([HumanMessage(content=content)])
            summary_text = (getattr(resp, "content", "") or "").strip()
        except Exception:
            summary_text = ""

    # STM: Zusammenfassung injizieren, damit nachfolgende Turns sie sehen
    thread_id = str(chat_id or "")
    if thread_id and summary_text:
        try:
            set_summary(thread_id, summary_text)
        except Exception:
            pass

    # LTM: als conversation_summary speichern (falls möglich)
    if summary_text and (user_id or chat_id):
        try:
            ltm.upsert_memory(user=str(user_id or chat_id), chat_id=str(chat_id or user_id or ""), text=summary_text, kind="conversation_summary")
        except Exception:
            pass

    out = {**state, "phase": "summarize"}
    if summary_text:
        out["summary_text"] = summary_text
    return out


__all__ = ["summarize_node"]

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/summarize.py =====

from langchain_core.messages import AIMessage, HumanMessage

from ....llm_factory import get_llm
from ..memory_utils import set_summary
from ....tools import long_term_memory as ltm

            return content.strip()

        except Exception:
            pass

    if summary_text:
        out["summary_text"] = summary_text
    return out

===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/validate_answer.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/validate_answer.py
from __future__ import annotations

import math
from typing import Any, Dict, List
import structlog

from ..state import ConsultState

log = structlog.get_logger(__name__)

def _sigmoid(x: float) -> float:
    try:
        return 1.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-x))
    except Exception:
        return 0.5

def _confidence_from_docs(docs: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> float:
    """
    Grobe Konfidenzabschätzung aus RAG-Scores.
    Nutzt fused_score, sonst max(vector_score, keyword_score/100).
    Falls Score bereits [0..1], direkt verwenden – sonst sigmoid.
    """
    if not docs:
        return 0.15

    vals: List[float] = []
    for d in docs[:6]:
        vs = d.get("vector_score")
        ks = d.get("keyword_score")
        fs = d.get("fused_score")
        try:
            base = float(fs if fs is not None else max(float(vs or 0.0), float(ks or 0.0) / 100.0))
        except Exception:
            base = 0.0

        if 0.0 <= base <= 1.0:
            vals.append(base)
        else:
            vals.append(_sigmoid(base))

    conf = sum(vals) / max(1, len(vals))
    return max(0.05, min(0.98, conf))

def _top_source(d: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    return (d.get("source")
            or (d.get("metadata") or {}).get("source")
            or "")

def validate_answer(state: ConsultState) -> ConsultState:
    """
    Bewertet die Antwortqualität (Konfidenz/Quellen) und MERGT den State,
    ohne RAG-Felder zu verlieren.
    """
    retrieved_docs: List[Dict[str, Any]] = state.get("retrieved_docs") or state.get("docs") or []
    context: str = state.get("context") or ""

    conf = _confidence_from_docs(retrieved_docs)
    needs_more = bool(state.get("needs_more_params")) or conf < 0.35

    validation: Dict[str, Any] = {
        "n_docs": len(retrieved_docs),
        "confidence": round(conf, 3),
        "top_source": _top_source(retrieved_docs[0]) if retrieved_docs else "",
    }

    log.info(
        "validate_answer",
        confidence=validation["confidence"],
        needs_more_params=needs_more,
        n_docs=validation["n_docs"],
        top_source=validation["top_source"],
    )

    return {
        **state,
        "phase": "validate_answer",
        "validation": validation,
        "confidence": conf,
        "needs_more_params": needs_more,
        # explizit erhalten
        "retrieved_docs": retrieved_docs,
        "docs": retrieved_docs,
        "context": context,
    }

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/validate_answer.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/validate_answer.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/validate_answer.py
from __future__ import annotations

import math
from typing import Any, Dict, List
import structlog

from ..state import ConsultState

log = structlog.get_logger(__name__)

def _sigmoid(x: float) -> float:
    try:
        return 1.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-x))
    except Exception:
        return 0.5

def _confidence_from_docs(docs: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> float:
    """
    Grobe Konfidenzabschätzung aus RAG-Scores.
    Nutzt fused_score, sonst max(vector_score, keyword_score/100).
    Falls Score bereits [0..1], direkt verwenden – sonst sigmoid.
    """
    if not docs:
        return 0.15

    vals: List[float] = []
    for d in docs[:6]:
        vs = d.get("vector_score")
        ks = d.get("keyword_score")
        fs = d.get("fused_score")
        try:
            base = float(fs if fs is not None else max(float(vs or 0.0), float(ks or 0.0) / 100.0))
        except Exception:
            base = 0.0

        if 0.0 <= base <= 1.0:
            vals.append(base)
        else:
            vals.append(_sigmoid(base))

    conf = sum(vals) / max(1, len(vals))
    return max(0.05, min(0.98, conf))

def _top_source(d: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    return (d.get("source")
            or (d.get("metadata") or {}).get("source")
            or "")

def validate_answer(state: ConsultState) -> ConsultState:
    """
    Bewertet die Antwortqualität (Konfidenz/Quellen) und MERGT den State,
    ohne RAG-Felder zu verlieren.
    """
    retrieved_docs: List[Dict[str, Any]] = state.get("retrieved_docs") or state.get("docs") or []
    context: str = state.get("context") or ""

    conf = _confidence_from_docs(retrieved_docs)
    needs_more = bool(state.get("needs_more_params")) or conf < 0.35

    validation: Dict[str, Any] = {
        "n_docs": len(retrieved_docs),
        "confidence": round(conf, 3),
        "top_source": _top_source(retrieved_docs[0]) if retrieved_docs else "",
    }

    log.info(
        "validate_answer",
        confidence=validation["confidence"],
        needs_more_params=needs_more,
        n_docs=validation["n_docs"],
        top_source=validation["top_source"],
    )

    return {
        **state,
        "phase": "validate_answer",
        "validation": validation,
        "confidence": conf,
        "needs_more_params": needs_more,
        # explizit erhalten
        "retrieved_docs": retrieved_docs,
        "docs": retrieved_docs,
        "context": context,
    }

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/validate_answer.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/validate.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/validate.py
from __future__ import annotations
from typing import Any, Dict


def _to_float(x: Any) -> Any:
    try:
        if isinstance(x, bool):
            return x
        return float(x)
    except Exception:
        return x


def validate_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """
    Leichter Parameter-Check/Normalisierung vor RAG.
    WICHTIG: Keine Berechnungen, kein Calculator-Aufruf – das macht calc_agent.
    """
    params = dict(state.get("params") or {})

    # numerische Felder best-effort in float wandeln
    for k in (
        "temp_max_c", "temp_min_c", "druck_bar", "drehzahl_u_min",
        "wellen_mm", "gehause_mm", "breite_mm",
        "relativgeschwindigkeit_ms",
        "tmax_c", "pressure_bar", "n_u_min", "rpm", "v_ms",
    ):
        if k in params and params[k] not in (None, "", []):
            params[k] = _to_float(params[k])

    # einfache Alias-Harmonisierung (falls Ziel noch leer)
    alias = {
        "tmax_c": "temp_max_c",
        "pressure_bar": "druck_bar",
        "n_u_min": "drehzahl_u_min",
        "rpm": "drehzahl_u_min",
        "v_ms": "relativgeschwindigkeit_ms",
    }
    for src, dst in alias.items():
        if (params.get(dst) in (None, "", [])) and (params.get(src) not in (None, "", [])):
            params[dst] = params[src]

    return {**state, "params": params, "phase": "validate"}

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/validate.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/nodes/validate.py =====

# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/state.py
from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, TypedDict
from typing_extensions import Annotated
from langchain_core.messages import AnyMessage
from langgraph.graph import add_messages


# ---- Parameter- & Derived-Typen -------------------------------------------------
class Parameters(TypedDict, total=False):
    # Kernparameter
    temp_max_c: float
    druck_bar: float
    drehzahl_u_min: float
    wellen_mm: float
    relativgeschwindigkeit_ms: float  # alias für geschwindigkeit_m_s
    geschwindigkeit_m_s: float
    # Hydraulik
    stange_mm: float
    nut_d_mm: float
    nut_b_mm: float
    # Aliasse / Harmonisierung
    tmax_c: float
    pressure_bar: float
    n_u_min: float
    rpm: float
    v_ms: float
    # optionale Filter/Routing
    material: str
    profile: str
    domain: str
    norm: str
    lang: str
    # optionale physikalische Parameter (falls bekannt; sonst werden optionale Berechnungen übersprungen)
    mu: float                     # Reibkoeffizient
    contact_pressure_mpa: float   # Kontaktpressung an der Dichtkante
    axial_force_n: float          # Axialkraft (Hydraulik)
    width_mm: float               # wirksame Dichtbreite (für Reib-/Leistungsabschätzung)


class Derived(TypedDict, total=False):
    # Allgemeine berechnete Größen
    surface_speed_m_s: float              # v
    umfangsgeschwindigkeit_m_s: float     # v (de)
    omega_rad_s: float                    # ω
    p_bar: float                          # Druck [bar]
    p_pa: float                           # Druck [Pa]
    p_mpa: float                          # Druck [MPa]
    pv_bar_ms: float                      # PV in bar·m/s
    pv_mpa_ms: float                      # PV in MPa·m/s
    # Optional – nur wenn genug Parameter vorliegen
    friction_force_n: float               # F_f = μ * N (wenn N/Kontaktpressung bekannt)
    friction_power_w: float               # P = F_f * v
    # Vorhandene Felder bleiben erhalten
    relativgeschwindigkeit_ms: float
    calculated: Dict[str, Any]
    flags: Dict[str, Any]
    warnings: List[str]
    requirements: List[str]


# ---- Graph-State ----------------------------------------------------------------
class ConsultState(TypedDict, total=False):
    # Dialog
    messages: Annotated[List[AnyMessage], add_messages]
    query: str

    # Parameter
    params: Parameters
    derived: Derived

    # Routing / Kontext
    user_id: Optional[str]
    tenant: Optional[str]
    domain: Optional[str]
    phase: Optional[str]
    consult_required: Optional[bool]

    # User-Profil (aus Postgres)
    user_profile: Dict[str, Any]

    # ---- UI/Frontend-Integration ----
    ui_event: Dict[str, Any]
    missing_fields: List[str]

    # --- RAG-Ergebnis ---
    retrieved_docs: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    context: str

    # Empfehlungen / Ergebnis
    empfehlungen: List[Dict[str, Any]]

    # Qualitäts-/Validierungsinfos
    validation: Dict[str, Any]
    confidence: float
    needs_more_params: bool

    # --- Legacy-Felder ---
    docs: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    citations: List[str]
    answer: Optional[str]

===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/state.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/state.py =====

    stange_mm: float
    nut_d_mm: float
    nut_b_mm: float

    # Qualitäts-/Validierungsinfos

    confidence: float

    # --- Legacy-Felder ---

===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/utils/graph_helpers.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/utils/graph_helpers.py
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from typing import Any, Dict, List

from .. import utils as utils_mod
from ..config import MAX_REVISE_COUNT, CRITIQUE_THRESHOLD, DOMAINS

log = logging.getLogger("uvicorn.error")

def _join_user_text(msgs: List) -> str:
    out: List[str] = []
    for m in msgs:
        role = (getattr(m, "type", "") or getattr(m, "role", "")).lower()
        content = getattr(m, "content", "")
        if isinstance(m, dict):
            role = (m.get("type") or m.get("role") or "").lower()
            content = m.get("content")
        if role in ("human", "user") and isinstance(content, str) and content.strip():
            out.append(content.strip())
    return "\n".join(out)

def _merge_seed_first(seed: Dict[str, Any], llm_out: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    out = dict(llm_out or {})
    for k, v in (seed or {}).items():
        if v not in (None, "", []):
            out[k] = v
    return out

def _compact_param_summary(domain: str, params: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    p = params or {}
    parts: List[str] = []

    domain_config = DOMAINS.get(domain, {})
    if domain_config:
        parts.append(domain_config.get('name', domain.upper()))
        if domain == "rwdr":
            if p.get("abmessung"):
                parts.append(str(p["abmessung"]))
            elif p.get("wellen_mm") and p.get("gehause_mm") and p.get("breite_mm"):
                parts.append(f'{p["wellen_mm"]}x{p["gehause_mm"]}x{p["breite_mm"]}')
    else:
        parts.append(domain.upper())

    if p.get("medium"):
        parts.append(str(p["medium"]))
    if p.get("temp_max_c") or p.get("tmax_c"):
        parts.append(f'Tmax {int(p.get("temp_max_c") or p.get("tmax_c"))} °C')
    if p.get("druck_bar"):
        parts.append(f'Druck {p["druck_bar"]} bar')
    if p.get("drehzahl_u_min"):
        parts.append(f'{int(p["drehzahl_u_min"])} U/min')
    if p.get("relativgeschwindigkeit_ms") or p.get("geschwindigkeit_m_s"):
        v = p.get("relativgeschwindigkeit_ms") or p.get("geschwindigkeit_m_s")
        parts.append(f'v≈{float(v):.2f} m/s')

    bl = p.get("material_blacklist") or p.get("vermeide_materialien")
    wl = p.get("material_whitelist") or p.get("bevorzugte_materialien")
    if bl:
        parts.append(f'Vermeide: {bl}')
    if wl:
        parts.append(f'Bevorzugt: {wl}')

    return ", ".join(parts)

# Node functions
def _extract_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    from ..extract import extract_params_with_llm
    from ..heuristic_extract import pre_extract_params

    try:
        msgs = utils_mod.normalize_messages(state.get("messages", []))
        params = dict(state.get("params") or {})
        user_text = _join_user_text(msgs)

        heur = pre_extract_params(user_text)
        seed = {**params, **{k: v for k, v in heur.items() if v not in (None, "", [])}}

        llm_params = extract_params_with_llm(user_text)
        final_params = _merge_seed_first(seed, llm_params)
        return {**state, "params": final_params, "phase": "extract"}
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[extract_node] Error: %s", e)
        return {**state, "phase": "extract", "error": str(e)}

def _compute_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    from ..domain_runtime import compute_domain

    try:
        domain = (state.get("domain") or "rwdr").strip().lower()
        params = dict(state.get("params") or {})
        derived = compute_domain(domain, params) or {}

        alias_map = {
            "tmax_c": params.get("temp_max_c"),
            "temp_c": params.get("temp_max_c"),
            "druck": params.get("druck_bar"),
            "pressure_bar": params.get("druck_bar"),
            "n_u_min": params.get("drehzahl_u_min"),
            "rpm": params.get("drehzahl_u_min"),
            "v_ms": params.get("relativgeschwindigkeit_ms") or params.get("geschwindigkeit_m_s"),
        }
        for k, v in alias_map.items():
            if k not in params and v not in (None, "", []):
                params[k] = v

        return {**state, "params": params, "derived": derived, "phase": "compute"}
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[compute_node] Error: %s", e)
        return {**state, "phase": "compute", "error": str(e)}

def _prepare_query_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    try:
        if (state.get("query") or "").strip():
            return {**state, "phase": "prepare_query"}

        params = dict(state.get("params") or {})
        domain = (state.get("domain") or "rwdr").strip().lower()

        user_text = ""  # Query technisch – kompakter Param-String
        param_str = _compact_param_summary(domain, params)
        prefix = DOMAINS.get(domain, {}).get("name", domain.upper())
        query = ", ".join([s for s in [prefix, user_text, param_str] if s])

        new_state = dict(state)
        new_state["query"] = query
        return {**new_state, "phase": "prepare_query"}
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[prepare_query_node] Error: %s", e)
        return {**state, "phase": "prepare_query", "error": str(e)}

def _respond_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    return {**state, "phase": "respond"}

def _bump_revise_count_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    metrics = dict(state.get("metrics") or {})
    metrics["revise_count"] = int(metrics.get("revise_count", 0)) + 1
    new_state = dict(state)
    new_state["metrics"] = metrics
    return new_state

# Conditional helpers
def _route_key(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    branch = (state.get("route") or "default").strip().lower() or "default"
    log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "lite_router", "route", branch, state)
    state["metrics"] = state.get("metrics", {}) | {"route_confidence": 1.0}
    return branch

def _intent_key(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    r = (state.get("route") or "").strip().lower()
    branch = "smalltalk" if r in {"chitchat", "smalltalk"} else "default"
    log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "intent_router", "intent", branch, state)
    return branch

def _ask_or_ok(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    p = state.get("params") or {}

    def has(v: Any) -> bool:
        if v is None:
            return False
        if isinstance(v, (list, dict)) and not v:
            return False
        if isinstance(v, str) and not v.strip():
            return False
        return True

    base_ok = has(p.get("temp_max_c")) and has(p.get("druck_bar"))
    rel_ok = has(p.get("relativgeschwindigkeit_ms") or p.get("geschwindigkeit_m_s")) or (
        has(p.get("wellen_mm")) and has(p.get("drehzahl_u_min"))
    )

    branch = "ask" if not (base_ok and rel_ok) else "ok"
    log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "ask_missing", "ask_or_ok", branch, state)
    return branch

def _after_rag(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    p = state.get("params") or {}

    def has(v: Any) -> bool:
        if v is None:
            return False
        if isinstance(v, (list, dict)) and not v:
            return False
        if isinstance(v, str) and not v.strip():
            return False
        return True

    base_ok = has(p.get("temp_max_c")) and has(p.get("druck_bar"))
    rel_ok = has(p.get("relativgeschwindigkeit_ms") or p.get("geschwindigkeit_m_s")) or (
        has(p.get("wellen_mm")) and has(p.get("drehzahl_u_min"))
    )
    docs = state.get("retrieved_docs") or state.get("docs") or []
    ctx_ok = bool(docs) or bool(state.get("context"))

    branch = "recommend" if (base_ok, rel_ok, ctx_ok) == (True, True, True) else "explain"
    log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "rag", "after_rag", branch, state)
    return branch

def _critique_key(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    # Falls nach der Antwort-Validierung noch Pflichtangaben fehlen → zurück zu ask_missing
    if state.get("needs_more_params"):
        branch = "ask_missing"
        log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "critique", "decision", branch, state)
        return branch

    critique_score = state.get("critique_score", 0.0)
    metrics = dict(state.get("metrics") or {})
    revise_count = int(metrics.get("revise_count", 0))

    # Hartes Limit für Revisionsrunden
    if revise_count >= MAX_REVISE_COUNT:
        branch = "ok"
    else:
        branch = "revise" if critique_score < CRITIQUE_THRESHOLD else "ok"

    log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "critique", "decision", branch, state)
    state["metrics"] = metrics | {"debate_delta": abs(1.0 - critique_score)}
    return branch

def _after_validate_answer(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    """
    Routing nach validate_answer:
      - Wenn Pflichtangaben fehlen → ask_missing
      - Wenn unsicher und wir haben noch Revisionsbudget → critique
      - Sonst direkt antworten
    """
    if state.get("needs_more_params"):
        decision = "ask_missing"
    else:
        conf = float(state.get("confidence") or state.get("answer_confidence") or 0.0)
        revise_count = int((state.get("metrics") or {}).get("revise_count", 0))
        decision = "critique" if (conf < 0.6 and revise_count < MAX_REVISE_COUNT) else "respond"
    log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "validate_answer", "next", decision, state)
    return decision

# Need to import log_branch_decision
from ...logging_utils import log_branch_decision
_GRAPH_NAME = "ConsultGraph"
===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/utils/graph_helpers.py =====


===== BEGIN backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/utils/graph_helpers.py =====
# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/utils/graph_helpers.py
from __future__ import annotations

import logging
from typing import Any, Dict, List

from .. import utils as utils_mod
from ..config import MAX_REVISE_COUNT, CRITIQUE_THRESHOLD, DOMAINS

log = logging.getLogger("uvicorn.error")

def _join_user_text(msgs: List) -> str:
    out: List[str] = []
    for m in msgs:
        role = (getattr(m, "type", "") or getattr(m, "role", "")).lower()
        content = getattr(m, "content", "")
        if isinstance(m, dict):
            role = (m.get("type") or m.get("role") or "").lower()
            content = m.get("content")
        if role in ("human", "user") and isinstance(content, str) and content.strip():
            out.append(content.strip())
    return "\n".join(out)

def _merge_seed_first(seed: Dict[str, Any], llm_out: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    out = dict(llm_out or {})
    for k, v in (seed or {}).items():
        if v not in (None, "", []):
            out[k] = v
    return out

def _compact_param_summary(domain: str, params: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    p = params or {}
    parts: List[str] = []

    domain_config = DOMAINS.get(domain, {})
    if domain_config:
        parts.append(domain_config.get('name', domain.upper()))
        if domain == "rwdr":
            if p.get("abmessung"):
                parts.append(str(p["abmessung"]))
            elif p.get("wellen_mm") and p.get("gehause_mm") and p.get("breite_mm"):
                parts.append(f'{p["wellen_mm"]}x{p["gehause_mm"]}x{p["breite_mm"]}')
    else:
        parts.append(domain.upper())

    if p.get("medium"):
        parts.append(str(p["medium"]))
    if p.get("temp_max_c") or p.get("tmax_c"):
        parts.append(f'Tmax {int(p.get("temp_max_c") or p.get("tmax_c"))} °C')
    if p.get("druck_bar"):
        parts.append(f'Druck {p["druck_bar"]} bar')
    if p.get("drehzahl_u_min"):
        parts.append(f'{int(p["drehzahl_u_min"])} U/min')
    if p.get("relativgeschwindigkeit_ms") or p.get("geschwindigkeit_m_s"):
        v = p.get("relativgeschwindigkeit_ms") or p.get("geschwindigkeit_m_s")
        parts.append(f'v≈{float(v):.2f} m/s')

    bl = p.get("material_blacklist") or p.get("vermeide_materialien")
    wl = p.get("material_whitelist") or p.get("bevorzugte_materialien")
    if bl:
        parts.append(f'Vermeide: {bl}')
    if wl:
        parts.append(f'Bevorzugt: {wl}')

    return ", ".join(parts)

# Node functions
def _extract_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    from ..extract import extract_params_with_llm
    from ..heuristic_extract import pre_extract_params

    try:
        msgs = utils_mod.normalize_messages(state.get("messages", []))
        params = dict(state.get("params") or {})
        user_text = _join_user_text(msgs)

        heur = pre_extract_params(user_text)
        seed = {**params, **{k: v for k, v in heur.items() if v not in (None, "", [])}}

        llm_params = extract_params_with_llm(user_text)
        final_params = _merge_seed_first(seed, llm_params)
        return {**state, "params": final_params, "phase": "extract"}
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[extract_node] Error: %s", e)
        return {**state, "phase": "extract", "error": str(e)}

def _compute_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    from ..domain_runtime import compute_domain

    try:
        domain = (state.get("domain") or "rwdr").strip().lower()
        params = dict(state.get("params") or {})
        derived = compute_domain(domain, params) or {}

        alias_map = {
            "tmax_c": params.get("temp_max_c"),
            "temp_c": params.get("temp_max_c"),
            "druck": params.get("druck_bar"),
            "pressure_bar": params.get("druck_bar"),
            "n_u_min": params.get("drehzahl_u_min"),
            "rpm": params.get("drehzahl_u_min"),
            "v_ms": params.get("relativgeschwindigkeit_ms") or params.get("geschwindigkeit_m_s"),
        }
        for k, v in alias_map.items():
            if k not in params and v not in (None, "", []):
                params[k] = v

        return {**state, "params": params, "derived": derived, "phase": "compute"}
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[compute_node] Error: %s", e)
        return {**state, "phase": "compute", "error": str(e)}

def _prepare_query_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    try:
        if (state.get("query") or "").strip():
            return {**state, "phase": "prepare_query"}

        params = dict(state.get("params") or {})
        domain = (state.get("domain") or "rwdr").strip().lower()

        user_text = ""  # Query technisch – kompakter Param-String
        param_str = _compact_param_summary(domain, params)
        prefix = DOMAINS.get(domain, {}).get("name", domain.upper())
        query = ", ".join([s for s in [prefix, user_text, param_str] if s])

        new_state = dict(state)
        new_state["query"] = query
        return {**new_state, "phase": "prepare_query"}
    except Exception as e:
        log.error("[prepare_query_node] Error: %s", e)
        return {**state, "phase": "prepare_query", "error": str(e)}

def _respond_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    return {**state, "phase": "respond"}

def _bump_revise_count_node(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    metrics = dict(state.get("metrics") or {})
    metrics["revise_count"] = int(metrics.get("revise_count", 0)) + 1
    new_state = dict(state)
    new_state["metrics"] = metrics
    return new_state

# Conditional helpers
def _route_key(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    branch = (state.get("route") or "default").strip().lower() or "default"
    log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "lite_router", "route", branch, state)
    state["metrics"] = state.get("metrics", {}) | {"route_confidence": 1.0}
    return branch

def _intent_key(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    r = (state.get("route") or "").strip().lower()
    branch = "smalltalk" if r in {"chitchat", "smalltalk"} else "default"
    log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "intent_router", "intent", branch, state)
    return branch

def _ask_or_ok(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    p = state.get("params") or {}

    def has(v: Any) -> bool:
        if v is None:
            return False
        if isinstance(v, (list, dict)) and not v:
            return False
        if isinstance(v, str) and not v.strip():
            return False
        return True

    base_ok = has(p.get("temp_max_c")) and has(p.get("druck_bar"))
    rel_ok = has(p.get("relativgeschwindigkeit_ms") or p.get("geschwindigkeit_m_s")) or (
        has(p.get("wellen_mm")) and has(p.get("drehzahl_u_min"))
    )

    branch = "ask" if not (base_ok and rel_ok) else "ok"
    log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "ask_missing", "ask_or_ok", branch, state)
    return branch

def _after_rag(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    p = state.get("params") or {}

    def has(v: Any) -> bool:
        if v is None:
            return False
        if isinstance(v, (list, dict)) and not v:
            return False
        if isinstance(v, str) and not v.strip():
            return False
        return True

    base_ok = has(p.get("temp_max_c")) and has(p.get("druck_bar"))
    rel_ok = has(p.get("relativgeschwindigkeit_ms") or p.get("geschwindigkeit_m_s")) or (
        has(p.get("wellen_mm")) and has(p.get("drehzahl_u_min"))
    )
    docs = state.get("retrieved_docs") or state.get("docs") or []
    ctx_ok = bool(docs) or bool(state.get("context"))

    branch = "recommend" if (base_ok, rel_ok, ctx_ok) == (True, True, True) else "explain"
    log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "rag", "after_rag", branch, state)
    return branch

def _critique_key(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    # Falls nach der Antwort-Validierung noch Pflichtangaben fehlen → zurück zu ask_missing
    if state.get("needs_more_params"):
        branch = "ask_missing"
        log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "critique", "decision", branch, state)
        return branch

    critique_score = state.get("critique_score", 0.0)
    metrics = dict(state.get("metrics") or {})
    revise_count = int(metrics.get("revise_count", 0))

    # Hartes Limit für Revisionsrunden
    if revise_count >= MAX_REVISE_COUNT:
        branch = "ok"
    else:
        branch = "revise" if critique_score < CRITIQUE_THRESHOLD else "ok"

    log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "critique", "decision", branch, state)
    state["metrics"] = metrics | {"debate_delta": abs(1.0 - critique_score)}
    return branch

def _after_validate_answer(state: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    """
    Routing nach validate_answer:
      - Wenn Pflichtangaben fehlen → ask_missing
      - Wenn unsicher und wir haben noch Revisionsbudget → critique
      - Sonst direkt antworten
    """
    if state.get("needs_more_params"):
        decision = "ask_missing"
    else:
        conf = float(state.get("confidence") or state.get("answer_confidence") or 0.0)
        revise_count = int((state.get("metrics") or {}).get("revise_count", 0))
        decision = "critique" if (conf < 0.6 and revise_count < MAX_REVISE_COUNT) else "respond"
    log_branch_decision(_GRAPH_NAME, "validate_answer", "next", decision, state)
    return decision

# Need to import log_branch_decision
from ...logging_utils import log_branch_decision
_GRAPH_NAME = "ConsultGraph"

# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/utils/parsing.py
from __future__ import annotations

import json
import re
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

from app.services.langgraph.prompting import strip_json_fence

def _split_items(text: str) -> List[str]:
    if not text:
        return []
    items = re.split(r'[•\-*]\s*', text.strip())
    return [item.strip() for item in items if item.strip()]

def _extract_json_any(s: str) -> str:
    s = (s or "").strip()
    if not s:
        return ""
    if (s[:1] in "{[") and (s[-1:] in "}]"):
        return s
    s2 = strip_json_fence(s)
    if (s2[:1] in "{[") and (s2[-1:] in "}]"):
        return s2
    m = re.search(r"\{(?:[^{}]|(?R))*\}", s, re.S)
    if m:
        return m.group(0)
    m = re.search(r"\[(?:[^\[\]]|(?R))*\]", s, re.S)
    return m.group(0) if m else ""

def _parse_empfehlungen(raw: str) -> Optional[List[Dict[str, Any]]]:
    if not raw:
        return None
    try:
        data = json.loads(strip_json_fence(raw))
        if isinstance(data, dict) and isinstance(data.get("empfehlungen"), list):
            return data["empfehlungen"]
    except Exception:
        pass
    return None

_RX = {
    "typ": re.compile(r"(?im)^\s*Typ:\s*(.+?)\s*$"),
    "werkstoff": re.compile(r"(?im)^\s*Werkstoff:\s*(.+?)\s*$"),
    "vorteile": re.compile(
        r"(?is)\bVorteile:\s*(.+?)(?:\n\s*(?:Einschr[aä]nkungen|Begr[üu]ndung|Abgeleiteter|Alternativen)\b|$)"
    ),
    "einschraenkungen": re.compile(
        r"(?is)\bEinschr[aä]nkungen:\s*(.+?)(?:\n\s*(?:Begr[üu]ndung|Abgeleiteter|Alternativen)\b|$)"
    ),
    "begruendung": re.compile(
        r"(?is)\bBegr[üu]ndung:\s*(.+?)(?:\n\s*(?:Abgeleiteter|Alternativen)\b|$)"
    ),
}

def _coerce_from_markdown(text: str) -> Optional[List[Dict[str, Any]]]:
    if not text:
        return None
    def _m(rx):
        m = rx.search(text)
        return (m.group(1).strip() if m else "")
    typ = _m(_RX["typ"])
    werkstoff = _m(_RX["werkstoff"])
    vorteile = _split_items(_m(_RX["vorteile"]))
    einschr = _split_items(_m(_RX["einschraenkungen"]))
    begr = _m(_RX["begruendung"])
    if not (typ or werkstoff or begr or vorteile or einschr):
        return None
    return [{
        "typ": typ or "",
        "werkstoff": werkstoff or "",
        "begruendung": begr or "",
        "vorteile": vorteile or [],
        "einschraenkungen": einschr or [],
        "geeignet_fuer": [],
    }]

def parse_recommendations(raw: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """
    Parses recommendations from raw LLM output.
    Tries JSON first, then markdown fallback.
    """
    json_snippet = _extract_json_any(raw)
    recs = _parse_empfehlungen(json_snippet) or _parse_empfehlungen(raw)
    if not recs:
        recs = _coerce_from_markdown(raw)
    if not recs:
        recs = [{
            "typ": "",
            "werkstoff": "",
            "begruendung": (raw[:600] if raw else "Keine strukturierte Empfehlung erhalten."),
            "vorteile": [],
            "einschraenkungen": [],
            "geeignet_fuer": [],
        }]
    return recs
===== END backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/utils/parsing.py =====

# backend/app/services/langgraph/graph/consult/utils/parsing.py
from __future__ import annotations

import json
import re
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

from app.services.langgraph.prompting import strip_json_fence

def _split_items(text: str) -> List[str]:
    if not text:
        return []
    items = re.split(r'[•\-*]\s*', text.strip())
    return [item.strip() for item in items if item.strip()]

def _extract_json_any(s: str) -> str:
    s = (s or "").strip()
    if not s:
        return ""
    if (s[:1] in "{[") and (s[-1:] in "}]"):
        return s
    s2 = strip_json_fence(s)
    if (s2[:1] in "{[") and (s2[-1:] in "}]"):
        return s2
    m = re.search(r"\{(?:[^{}]|(?R))*\}", s, re.S)
    if m:
        return m.group(0)
    m = re.search(r"\[(?:[^\[\]]|(?R))*\]", s, re.S)
    return m.group(0) if m else ""

def _parse_empfehlungen(raw: str) -> Optional[List[Dict[str, Any]]]:

        return None
    try:
        data = json.loads(strip_json_fence(raw))
        if isinstance(data, dict) and isinstance(data.get("empfehlungen"), list):
            return data["empfehlungen"]
    except Exception:
        pass
    return None

    "typ": re.compile(r"(?im)^\s*Typ:\s*(.+?)\s*$"),
    "werkstoff": re.compile(r"(?im)^\s*Werkstoff:\s*(.+?)\s*$"),
    "vorteile": re.compile(
        r"(?is)\bVorteile:\s*(.+?)(?:\n\s*(?:Einschr[aä]nkungen|Begr[üu]ndung|Abgeleiteter|Alternativen)\b|$)"
    ),
    "einschraenkungen": re.compile(
        r"(?is)\bEinschr[aä]nkungen:\s*(.+?)(?:\n\s*(?:Begr[üu]ndung|Abgeleiteter|Alternativen)\b|$)"
    ),
    "begruendung": re.compile(
        r"(?is)\bBegr[üu]ndung:\s*(.+?)(?:\n\s*(?:Abgeleiteter|Alternativen)\b|$)"
    ),
}

def _coerce_from_markdown(text: str) -> Optional[List[Dict[str, Any]]]:

        return None

        m = rx.search(text)

def parse_recommendations(raw: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:

    return recs
